### [1] [An Empirical Study of LLM-Generated Specifications for VeriFast](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26490v1)
*Wen Fan,Minh Tran,Sanya Dod,Xin Hu,Marilyn Rego,Danning Xie,Jenna DiVincenzo,Lin Tan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了LLM为SL验证器VeriFast生成规范的能力，发现功能保持良好但验证成功率仅31.4%，主要错误源于领域知识缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM应用主要针对非SL验证器，而SL验证器需要复杂辅助规范，因此有必要评估LLM在SL规范生成上的表现。

Method: 使用8种提示方法、10种LLM、3种输入类型，分两阶段评估303个C函数与VeriFast的规范生成，并进行定量和定性分析。

Result: LLM在源代码和规范中功能行为保持率均>91%，但验证成功率仅31.4%；Gemini 2.5 Pro和提供形式化契约能提高成功率；94%的错误源于LLM对SL领域知识的不足。

Conclusion: 这些发现为优化LLM生成SL验证器规范提供了指导，强调了领域知识的重要性。

中文摘要：静态验证工具可以确保工业规模的软件，但需要大量的人力来编写规范。对于基于分离逻辑的静态验证器（SL验证器）尤其如此，它们擅长验证堆操作程序，但需要许多复杂的辅助规范来推理堆结构。最近的研究应用大型语言模型（LLM）生成代码、测试和证明，包括用于验证器的规范，但主要针对非SL验证器。为了解决这一差距，本文全面评估了LLM在被提示为使用SL验证器VeriFast验证303个C函数生成规范时的表现。我们分两个阶段探索了八种提示方法、十种LLM和三种输入类型。使用定量和定性分析来评估LLM生成的代码和规范的功能行为、可验证性和错误。结果表明，LLM在源代码和规范中保持了功能行为（均超过91%），但验证成功率中等（31.4%）。使用Gemini 2.5 Pro并提供形式化契约在我们的设置中导致了更高的成功率。此外，大多数错误（94%）来自LLM在SL验证器（如VeriFast）的领域特定知识上的错误。这些发现为优化针对SL验证器的LLM生成规范提供了指导。

Original abstract: Static verification tools can assure industrial scale software, but require significant human labor to write specifications. This is particularly true of static verifiers based on separation logic (SL verifiers), which excel at verifying heapmanipulating programs, but require many complex auxiliary specifications to reason about heap structure. Recent work applies large language models (LLMs) to generate code, tests, and proofs, including specifications for verifiers, but mostly targeting non-SL verifiers. To address this gap, this paper thoroughly evaluates how well LLMs perform when prompted to generate specifications for verifying 303 C functions with the SL verifier VeriFast. We explored eight prompting approaches, ten LLMs, and three input types in two stages. Quantitative and qualitative analyses are used to assess the LLM-generated code and specifications for functional behavior, verifiability and errors. The results show that LLMs preserve functional behavior in source code and specifications (both over 91%), but achieve modest verification success (31.4%). Using Gemini 2.5 Pro and providing formal contracts lead to higher success rates in our setting. Moreover, most errors (94%) come from LLMs' mistakes in the domainspecific knowledge of SL verifiers such as VeriFast. These findings provide guidance for optimizing LLM-generated specifications for SL verifiers.

</details>


### [2] [Evaluation-Strategy Gap in Fault Diagnosis of Deep Learning Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26492v1)
*Sigma Jahan*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 深度学习故障诊断技术在不同程序间存在0.190的准确率差距，该差距源于程序级特征结构，曲率特征对未见过程序有效，而优化器与激活特征仅适用于训练见过的程序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有故障诊断技术多采用程序内交叉验证评估，可能不适用于未见过程序，需量化性能差距并分析原因。

Method: 使用DynFault语料库进行实验，对比程序内评估与整体程序留出评估，分析特征集（曲率、优化器、激活）对性能的影响。

Result: 程序间评估存在0.190的平衡准确率差距，差距源于程序级结构；曲率特征在未见过程序上表现良好，而优化器和激活特征仅在训练期间见过的程序上有效。

Conclusion: 故障诊断技术需考虑程序级特征分布差异，曲率特征有望提升跨程序泛化能力。

中文摘要：深度学习程序在训练期间可能因多种原因失败，诊断原因是一项成本高昂且耗时的维护任务。用于诊断此类失败的技术通常通过程序内交叉验证进行评估，这对于涉及未见过程序的部署设置可能不充分。因此，有必要评估这些设置下的性能差异，并确定已建立的深度学习故障诊断技术中任何性能差距的原因。我们使用DynFault（一个包含来自38个真实世界深度学习程序的5,542条故障注入训练轨迹的语料库）研究了这一差距。我们发现，在程序内评估与整体程序留出之间，现有故障诊断技术的平衡准确率差距为0.190。我们还发现，差距来自于特征中的程序级结构，这促使我们检查两个运行时特征集——曲率特征和优化器特征——及其在未见过程序上的行为。我们发现，曲率特征对于未见过程序的不稳定性检测有用，而优化器和激活特征仅对训练期间见过的程序有帮助。

Original abstract: Deep Learning (DL) programs can fail during training for many reasons, and diagnosing the cause is a costly and time-consuming maintenance task. Techniques for diagnosing such failures are commonly assessed using within-program cross-validation, which may be inadequate for deployment settings involving previously unseen programs. It is therefore necessary to assess how performance differs across these settings and to identify the causes of any performance gap in established fault diagnosis techniques for DL. We investigate this gap using DynFault, a corpus of 5,542 fault-injected training traces from 38 real-world DL programs. We found a gap of 0.190 in balanced accuracy for existing fault diagnosis techniques between within-program evaluation and holding out whole programs. We also found the gap comes from program-level structure in the features, which led us to examine two runtime feature sets, curvature features and optimizer features, and their behavior on unseen programs. We found that curvature features are useful for instability detection on unseen programs, while optimizer and activation features help only on programs seen during training.

</details>


### [3] [Same Scrutiny, More Time: Eye Tracking Insights into Reviewing LLM-Labelled Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26505v1)
*Ranim Khojah,Francisco Gomes de Oliveira Neto,Mazen Mohamad,Julian Frattini,Philipp Leitner*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过Wizard-of-Oz实验发现，标记为LLM生成的代码虽然不会改变审查的彻底性，但会吸引更多注视时间，并且开发者会调整审查策略（如关注逻辑正确性或使用提示）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究开发者实际审查LLM生成代码时的行为，因为现有建议与可能的行为之间存在差距，且该领域尚未被充分探索。

Method: 采用Wizard-of-Oz实验，结合眼动追踪和退出访谈收集数据，使用贝叶斯数据分析和定性分析。

Result: 参与者对LLM标记代码的审查彻底性不变，但注视时间增加；开发者调整策略，关注逻辑正确性或用提示指导审查。

Conclusion: 揭示了意图与行为之间的差距，建议软件公司重新审视AI政策以支持更好的审查实践。

中文摘要：现代软件开发日益涉及使用大型语言模型（LLM）生成代码。尽管这些模型发展迅速，但它们仍然容易出错和产生幻觉，因此强调了仔细检查代码的重要性。然而，在实践中，开发人员对LLM生成代码的信任程度以及他们彻底审查的意愿可能与这些建议有所不同。开发人员在实际审查LLM生成代码时的行为在很大程度上仍未得到探索。在本研究中，我们进行了一项Wizard-of-Oz实验，以考察软件工程师在代码审查任务中，当代码明确标记为LLM生成时的行为。我们通过眼动追踪和退出访谈收集了行为数据和参与者反馈。结合贝叶斯数据分析与定性分析，我们发现虽然参与者代码审查的彻底性没有改变，但他们花费更多时间注视标记为LLM的代码，表明标签本身会影响注意力。从业者还通过基于特定标准（如逻辑正确性）评估代码或使用提示来指导审查，从而调整了他们对LLM标记代码的审查策略。这些发现为基于LLM的工具设计提供了关于标记以及将提示作为软件工件纳入的启示。我们的研究揭示了审查者意图与实际审查行为之间的差距，强调了软件公司需要重新审视其AI政策（特别是关于LLM辅助开发的政策），以更好地支持开发人员审查LLM生成的代码。

Original abstract: Modern software development increasingly involves the use of large language models (LLMs) to generate code. Despite their rapid advancement, LLMs remain prone to errors and hallucinations, emphasizing the importance of careful code inspection. However, in practice, developers' trust in LLM-generated code and their willingness to review it thoroughly may differ from these recommendations. How developers actually behave when reviewing LLM-generated code remains largely unexplored. In this study, we conduct a Wizard-of-Oz experiment to examine how software engineers behave when code is explicitly labeled as LLM-generated during a code review task. We collect both behavioral data and participant feedback through eye-tracking and exit interviews. Combining Bayesian data analysis with qualitative analysis, we found that while the thoroughness of code review did not change for participants, they spent more time fixating on LLM-labelled code, indicating that the label itself influences attention. Practitioners also adapted their review strategy for LLM-labelled code by assessing the code based on specific criteria (e.g., logical correctness), or using the prompt to guide their review. These findings inform LLM-based tool design on labelling while incorporating the prompt as a software artifact. Our study reveals a gap between reviewers' intentions and actual reviewing behaviour, highlighting the need for software companies to revisit their AI policies (particularly regarding LLM-assisted development) to better support developers in reviewing LLM-generated code.

</details>


### [4] [ConcoLixir: Reactive LLM Discovery Oracles for Python Concolic Testing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26545v1)
*Dong Chen,Chih-Duo Hong,Fang Yu*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ConcoLixir通过LLM作为发现预言机，生成种子和具体输入，显著提升Python concolic测试的覆盖率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Python concolic测试面临库调用导致符号降级、语义操作难求解、探索停滞等限制，需要一种互补方法。

Method: 提出ConcoLixir，集成LLM作为发现预言机，在求解器失败时生成具体输入，在覆盖率停滞时针对未覆盖代码，候选通过concolic执行验证。

Result: 在合成、真实和库目标上，平均行覆盖率分别提升8.6、15.1和17.0个百分点，总API成本仅1.63美元。

Conclusion: 有界的LLM发现能有效补充符号推理，无需替代传统求解器。

中文摘要：Concolic测试结合了具体执行与符号约束求解，但Python程序暴露了反复出现的限制。库调用可能导致符号变量降级为具体值。正则表达式、校验和、解析器及其他语义操作可能难以求解，探索可能在已覆盖路径上停滞。我们提出了ConcoLixir，一种针对Python concolic执行的响应式LLM扩展。该LLM充当发现预言机，而非求解器或正确性预言机的替代品。它生成初始种子，在求解器失败后提出具体输入，并在覆盖率停滞时针对未覆盖代码。每个候选被concolically执行，仅观察到的覆盖率和收集的路径约束指导后续探索。在合成、真实世界和库目标上，与没有LLM预言机的基线concolic测试器相比，ConcoLixir将平均行覆盖率分别提高了8.6、15.1和17.0个百分点。收益在语义障碍和库边界附近最为显著，完整评估花费了1.63美元的API费用。这些结果表明，有界的LLM发现可以补充符号推理而无需取代它。

Original abstract: Concolic testing combines concrete execution with symbolic constraint solving, but Python programs expose recurring limits. Library calls can cause symbolic variables to downgrade to concrete values. Regular expressions, checksums, parsers, and other semantic operations can be hard to solve, and exploration can plateau on already covered paths. We present ConcoLixir, a reactive LLM extension for Python concolic execution. The LLM acts as a discovery oracle, not a replacement for the solver or a correctness oracle. It generates initial seeds, proposes concrete inputs after solver failures, and targets uncovered code when coverage stalls. Each candidate is executed concolically, and only observed coverage and collected path constraints guide later exploration. Across synthetic, real-world, and library targets, ConcoLixir improves mean line coverage over the baseline concolic tester without an LLM oracle by 8.6, 15.1, and 17.0 percentage points. The gains are strongest near semantic barriers and library boundaries, and the full evaluation costs \$1.63 in API charges. These results show that bounded LLM discovery can complement symbolic reasoning without replacing it.

</details>


### [5] [Quantum Mutant Equivalence via Transpilation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26604v1)
*José Campos,Andriy Miranskyy*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出基于转译器的等价性（TBE）方法，通过比较转译后的OpenQASM代码来识别量子变异体中的等价变异体，在348,299个存活变异体中以100%精确率和82%准确率识别出32.1%的等价变异体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变异测试中的等价变异体问题在量子软件中未得到解决，导致存活变异体无法区分是测试薄弱还是语义等价，浪费测试资源并扭曲评估结果。

Method: 提出基于转译器的等价性（TBE）方法，在同一配置下转译原始电路和变异电路，并比较它们生成的OpenQASM代码来判断语义等价。

Result: 在348,299个存活变异体中，92,011个为等价；TBE识别出29,536个（32.1%）为等价，精确率100%，准确率82%。

Conclusion: TBE方法能有效识别量子变异体中的等价变异体，具有高精确率和较好准确率，有助于提升量子变异测试的效率。

中文摘要：变异测试通过引入人工故障（变异体）并检查测试是否能够检测（杀死）它们来评估测试套件的质量。一个核心挑战是等价变异体问题：一些变异体在语法上与原程序不同，但在语义上与之相同，因此无法被任何测试杀死。如果不加以识别，这些变异体会浪费测试工作并扭曲变异得分。在量子软件中，变异测试正被越来越多地使用，但等价变异体问题仍未解决。最近的一项研究生成了超过70万个量子电路变异体，发现大约一半存活了可用测试，这使得不清楚这些存活变异体是反映了测试薄弱还是语义等价。我们提出了基于转译器的等价性（TBE）方法，这是一种轻量级方法，通过在同一配置下转译原始电路和变异电路，并比较它们生成的OpenQASM代码来识别等价的量子变异体。我们在348,299个存活变异体上评估了TBE，其中92,011个是等价的；TBE识别出其中29,536个（32.1%）为等价，同时实现了100%的精确率和82%的准确率。

Original abstract: Mutation testing evaluates test suite quality by introducing artificial faults (mutants) and checking whether tests detect (kill) them. A central challenge is the equivalent mutant problem: some mutants are syntactically different from the original program but semantically identical to it and therefore cannot be killed by any test. If left unidentified, such mutants waste testing effort and distort mutation scores. In quantum software, mutation testing is increasingly used, but the equivalent mutant problem remains unsolved. A recent study generated more than 700,000 quantum circuit mutants and found that roughly half survived the available tests, making it unclear whether these survivors reflect weak tests or semantic equivalence. We propose Transpiler-Based Equivalence (TBE), a lightweight approach that identifies equivalent quantum mutants by transpiling original and mutated circuits under the same configuration and comparing their resulting OpenQASM code. We evaluate TBE on 348,299 surviving mutants, 92,011 of which are equivalent; TBE identifies 29,536 of them (32.1%) as equivalent while achieving 100% precision and 82% accuracy.

</details>


### [6] [Knowledge-Based Pull Requests: A Trusted Workflow for Agent-Mediated Knowledge Collaboration](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26721v1)
*Xinyu Zhang,Weiwei Sun*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: KPR是一种分离知识接受与代码合并的代理中介协作工作流，旨在降低理解外部变更的成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编码代理使代码生成成本降低，但理解意图、协商范围和管理长期项目责任仍成本高昂，传统拉取请求将知识决策与实现决策混为一谈。

Method: 提出KPR工作流：将外部贡献视为知识来源，经提炼为人工确认的知识包，再由项目内部代理在受控环境中重新生成代码；并通过七个公共PR的模拟试点进行验证。

Result: 试点表明KPR包可从真实PR材料实例化，并在描述消融、差异消融和合成恶意补丁条件下通过压力测试。

Conclusion: KPR的价值在于通过可审计的提取、转换和项目端再生，降低理解与重做高上下文外部变更的成本，需进一步实证检验。

中文摘要：AI编码代理正在改变软件协作的瓶颈：代码越来越便宜，而理解意图、协商范围和管理长期项目责任仍然成本高昂。本文提出了基于知识的拉取请求（Knowledge-Based Pull Requests, KPR），这是一种可信的工作流，用于跨信任边界的代理中介软件协作，包括开源、企业、供应商、承包商和客户驱动场景。在KPR中，外部协作者的本地代码、测试和清理后的代理交互轨迹被视作知识来源，而非默认的合并候选。代理将这些来源提炼成人工确认的知识包，并将其转化为面向审阅者的形式，如设计备忘录、风险检查清单、测试计划或实施简报。项目拥有的内部可信编码代理随后在接收项目的环境中，根据仓库上下文、工程惯例、测试和安全策略重新生成候选代码。因此，KPR将传统拉取请求中经常合并的两个决策分离开来：知识是否应进入项目，以及特定实现是否应合并。我们贡献了KPR工作流、候选工件模式、成本核算视图、协作网关架构、一个基于七个已合并公共拉取请求的最小受控模拟试点，以及评估议程。试点表明，KPR包可以从真实PR材料中实例化，并在描述消融、差异消融和合成恶意补丁条件下进行压力测试。我们将KPR定位为一个可经验测试的工作流：其价值取决于可审计的提取、转换和项目端再生是否降低了理解和重做高上下文外部更改的成本。

Original abstract: AI coding agents are changing the bottleneck in software collaboration: code is increasingly cheap, while understanding intent, negotiating scope, and governing long-term project responsibility remain costly. This paper proposes \emph{Knowledge-Based Pull Requests} (KPR), a trusted workflow for agent-mediated software collaboration across trust boundaries, including open source, enterprise, vendor, contractor, and customer-driven settings. In KPR, an external collaborator's local code, tests, and cleaned agent interaction trace are treated as knowledge sources rather than as the default merge candidate. Agents distill these sources into a human-confirmed knowledge package and render it into reviewer-facing forms such as design memos, risk checklists, test plans, or implementation briefs. A project-owned inner trusted coding agent then regenerates candidate code inside the receiving project's environment under repository context, engineering conventions, tests, and security policy. KPR therefore separates two decisions that traditional pull requests often collapse: whether the knowledge should enter the project, and whether a particular implementation should be merged. We contribute the KPR workflow, a candidate artifact schema, a cost-accounting view, a collaboration gateway architecture, a minimal controlled simulation pilot over seven merged public pull requests, and an evaluation agenda. The pilot shows that KPR packages can be instantiated from real PR material and stress-tested under description ablation, diff ablation, and synthetic poisoned-patch conditions. We position KPR as an empirically testable workflow: its value depends on whether auditable extraction, transformation, and project-side regeneration reduce the cost of understanding and reworking high-context external changes.

</details>


### [7] [Towards Evaluation of Implicit Software World Models in Coding LLMs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27406v1)
*Egor Bogomolov,Yaroslav Zharov*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过预测执行资源（如内存、时间、分析器输出）来评估AI模型对软件执行的理解，发现所有模型表现不佳且脆弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试主要关注控制流，忽略了软件执行资源方面的理解，因此需要更广泛的评估来揭示AI模型在软件执行理解上的不足。

Method: 使用SWE-bench Verified数据集，在方法和行粒度上预测峰值内存、墙钟时间和排序后的分析器输出，同时评估测试结果和异常类。

Result: 所有测试模型（包括前沿模型）在预测执行资源方面表现一般且行为脆弱，表明缺乏对软件执行的理解。

Conclusion: AI模型对软件执行的理解远不如对源代码编写的理解，需要在训练和评估中加强对执行资源的考虑。

中文摘要：软件工程，无论是人类执行还是AI智能体执行，都需要推理软件的行为方式。我们将支持这种推理的内部模型称为软件世界模型，并认为当前代码执行基准测试覆盖了其中经过充分研究的一个方面——控制流。在本文中，我们通过将可观察轴转向执行资源，朝着更广泛的评估迈出了一步：除了测试结果和异常类之外，我们还预测了方法和行粒度的峰值内存、墙钟时间以及排序后的分析器输出。我们使用SWE-bench Verified作为数据源，以使测试贴近真实的软件工程任务。所有测试的模型，包括前沿模型，都表现出性能一般且行为脆弱，这表明它们在理解软件如何执行（而非源代码如何编写）方面存在显著不足。

Original abstract: Software engineering, whether performed by humans or by AI agents, requires reasoning about how software behaves. We call the internal model that supports such reasoning the software world model, and view current code-execution benchmarks as covering one well-studied slice of it -- control flow. In this paper, we take a step toward a broader evaluation by shifting the observable axis to execution resources: alongside test outcome and exception class, we predict peak memory, wall-clock time, and ranked profiler outputs at method and line granularity. We use SWE-bench Verified as the source of data to hold the test close to real-world software engineering tasks. All tested models, frontier ones included, show modest performance and brittle behaviour, suggesting a notable lack of understanding of how software is executed, as opposed to how its source code is written.

</details>


### [8] [A Deterministic Control Plane for LLM Coding Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26924v1)
*Padmaraj Madatha*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文研究LLM代理配置的普遍性问题，提出Rel(AI)Build系统作为确定性控制平面，通过内容寻址、权限管理、状态机等机制管理配置，确保安全与一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM代理配置缺乏管理，存在配置作为未声明共享组件传播、很少修订、权限边界声明不足等问题，需要确定性控制平面。

Method: 通过大规模调查（10,008个仓库）揭示问题，提出Rel(AI)Build系统，包括内容寻址、HMAC锁文件、审计日志、分层权限、阻止列表、阶段状态机、多IDE编译、提示漂移检测等机制。

Result: 调查发现10.1%的配置SHA-256重复，75.5%跨组织，58%单次提交，<1%声明权限。Rel(AI)Build的合规性测试确认各机制实施其不变量。

Conclusion: LLM代理配置需要确定性和工具无关的治理，不能依赖LLM编排，Rel(AI)Build提供了一组可行的机制，但开发者成果需未来研究。

中文摘要：LLM编码工具赋予代理广泛的文件和shell访问权限，然而引导它们的配置层——规则文件、代理定义、IDE特定的markdown——在很大程度上是未管理的。对10,008个公共GitHub仓库（n=6,145个代理配置文件）的普遍性研究发现，代理配置作为未声明的共享组件传播：10.1%的跟踪路径是跨独立仓库的SHA-256完全重复（经分叉调整、阈值无关），其中75.5%的克隆对跨越组织边界。另外两个模式具有指示性：配置很少被修订（58%为单次提交；年龄标准化后0.4 vs 0.6次提交/月，对比CI/CD工作流），并且很少声明权限边界（<1%的代理配置 vs 33%的Actions工作流，n=31个真阳性）。我们提出一个确定性控制平面，位于工具之上，与这些差距一一对应。Rel(AI)Build将代理定义视为托管供应链（SHA-256内容寻址、HMAC印章锁文件、哈希链审计日志）；在LLM调用前强制执行分层权限和攻击来源的阻止列表；通过具有需求到文件到测试可追溯性的阶段状态机来门控特性工作；将单个规范定义编译到七个IDE目标；并通过Jaccard相似性检测提示漂移。对注入违规的合规性测试确认每个机制执行其声明的不变量；开发者成果仍然是未来工作。这一层的治理必须是确定性的且与工具无关——不委托给进一步的LLM编排。

Original abstract: LLM coding harnesses grant agents broad file and shell access, yet the configuration layer that steers them -- rules files, agent definitions, IDE-specific markdown -- is largely unmanaged. A prevalence study of 10,008 public GitHub repositories (n=6,145 agent config files) finds that agent configurations propagate as undeclared shared components: 10.1% of tracked paths are SHA-256 exact duplicates across independent repositories (fork-adjusted, threshold-independent), with 75.5% of clone pairs crossing organisational boundaries. Two further patterns are indicative: configurations are rarely revised (58% single-commit; 0.4 vs 0.6 commits/month age-normalised against CI/CD workflows), and rarely declare permission boundaries (<1% of agent configs vs 33% of Actions workflows, n=31 true positives).
  We propose a deterministic control plane above the harness that maps one-to-one to these gaps. Rel(AI)Build treats agent definitions as a managed supply chain (SHA-256 content addressing, HMAC-stamped lockfiles, hash-chained audit logs); enforces tiered permissions and attack-derived blocklists before LLM invocation; gates feature work through a phase state machine with requirement-to-file-to-test traceability; compiles a single canonical definition to seven IDE targets; and detects prompt drift via Jaccard similarity. Conformance tests on injected violations confirm each mechanism enforces its stated invariant; developer outcomes remain future work. Governance of this layer must be deterministic and tool-agnostic -- not delegated to further LLM orchestration.

</details>


### [9] [Are LLMs Ready for Anti-Pattern Detection in Microservice Architectures?](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26927v1)
*Marco De Luca,Domenico Amalfitano,Porfirio Tramontana,Anna Rita Fasolino*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文评估了大语言模型用于微服务架构反模式检测的能力，发现其与传统静态分析相比各有优劣，但可作为一种补充工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微服务系统中架构反模式影响可维护性和质量，现有检测方法依赖静态分析，存在工具依赖、规则编码固定、难以适应异构仓库等问题，因此探索大语言模型作为替代或补充方案。

Method: 构建包含16种架构反模式的微服务仓库基准数据集，使用基于提示的分析管道，评估三个通用大语言模型，并与静态分析工具MARS进行精确率和召回率的对比。

Result: 大语言模型在局部、异构或语义丰富的反模式上表现具有竞争力，但在需要显式结构或跨服务依赖的反模式上不如静态分析。

Conclusion: 大语言模型尚不能替代传统静态分析，但可作为架构评估的补充工具，在特定场景下提供有用支持。

中文摘要：微服务系统容易出现反复出现的架构反模式，这些反模式会阻碍可维护性、可演化性和运行质量。现有的反模式检测方法大多依赖于静态分析和手工规则，这种方法虽然有效，但通常依赖于特定工具，仅限于显式编码的检测逻辑，并且难以适应异构仓库。在本文中，我们研究了大语言模型是否能够通过基于提示的分析管道对静态仓库工件进行分析，从而支持微服务架构中的架构反模式检测。我们在一个包含16种架构反模式注释的微服务仓库基准数据集上评估了三个通用大语言模型，并使用基于精确率和召回率的统一评估协议，将它们与最先进的静态分析工具MARS进行了比较。我们的结果表明，大语言模型可以为反模式检测提供有用的支持，在多个反模式上实现了具有竞争力的性能，尤其是在相关证据是局部、异构或语义丰富的情况下。同时，在需要显式结构或跨服务依赖证据的反模式上，它们表现出明显的局限性，而静态分析在这些方面仍然更可靠。这些发现表明，大语言模型尚不能替代传统分析器，但已经代表了微服务系统架构评估中一种有前途的补充辅助手段。

Original abstract: Microservice systems are prone to recurrent architectural anti-patterns (APs) that hinder maintainability, evolvability, and operational quality. Most existing AP detection approaches rely on static analysis and handcrafted rules, which can be effective but are often tool-dependent, limited to explicitly encoded detection logic, and difficult to adapt to heterogeneous repositories. In this paper, we investigate whether large language models (LLMs) are ready to support architectural anti-pattern detection in microservice architectures through a prompt-based analysis pipeline over static repository artifacts. We evaluate three general-purpose LLMs on a curated benchmark of microservice repositories annotated with 16 architectural anti-patterns, and compare their performance against the state-of-the-art static-analysis tool MARS using a uniform evaluation protocol based on precision and recall. Our results show that LLMs can provide useful support for anti-pattern detection, achieving competitive performance on several anti-patterns, especially when the relevant evidence is local, heterogeneous, or semantically rich. At the same time, they exhibit clear limitations on anti-patterns that require explicit structural or cross-service dependency evidence, where static analysis remains more reliable. These findings suggest that LLMs are not yet a replacement for traditional analyzers, but already represent a promising complementary aid for architectural assessment in microservice systems.

</details>


### [10] [CLIR: Liveness-Driven and Structure-Aware Fuzzing for the Cranelift Compiler](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26977v1)
*Shangtong Cao,Tianlei Song,Qiuping Yi,Tianyu Chen,Guoai Xu,Ningyu He,Haoyu Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: CLIR是一个差分测试框架，通过语法保持分层生成、活性引导指令细化和诊断引导跨架构适配，有效发现Cranelift编译器中的大量错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cranelift编译器测试面临三大挑战：构造严格SSA形式的有效IR、生成高计算密度序列以压力测试后端、平衡广泛后端覆盖与高效根因分析。

Method: 提出CLIR框架，包含语法保持的分层生成策略、活性引导的指令细化机制和诊断引导的跨架构适配方案。

Result: CLIR检测到比现有基线多8-24倍的独特错误，72小时内发现24个错误，21个已确认，9个已修复。

Conclusion: CLIR在测试Cranelift编译器方面显著优于现有方法，有效提升了缺陷检测效率和跨架构覆盖。

中文摘要：现代编译器是复杂的软件系统，必须正确地将高级编程语言翻译为跨多种架构的机器码。Cranelift 是一个快速且现代的编译器后端，最初为 WebAssembly 开发，最近被采纳为 Rust 的实验性后端，因其相比 LLVM 更优越的编译速度和全面的多架构支持（包括 x86-64、AArch64、s390x 和 RISCV64）而日益重要。然而，尽管编译器测试经过数十年的发展，测试 Cranelift 仍然面临独特挑战，包括：(1) 在严格强制 SSA 形式下构建有效的 IR，(2) 生成具有足够计算密度的序列以压力测试后端组件，以及 (3) 在异构架构中平衡广泛的后端覆盖与高效的根因分析。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了 CLIR，一个差分测试框架，集成了语法保持的分层生成策略以保证 SSA 有效性、活性引导的指令细化机制以最大化计算密度，以及诊断引导的跨架构适配方案以促进跨异构后端的有效根因分析。我们的全面评估表明，CLIR 显著优于现有最先进的基线，分别检测到比 cranelift-fuzzgen、wasm-smith 和 WASMaker 多 8 倍、24 倍和 8 倍的独特错误，而 RustSmith 未发现任何错误。因此，在 72 小时的测试中，CLIR 发现了涵盖所有目标架构的 24 个错误，其中 21 个已确认，9 个已修复。

Original abstract: Modern compilers are complex software systems that must correctly translate high-level programming languages into machine code across multiple architectures. Cranelift, a fast and modern compiler backend originally developed for WebAssembly and recently adopted as an experimental backend for Rust, has gained increasing importance due to its superior compilation speed compared to LLVM and comprehensive multi-architecture support, including x86-64, AArch64, s390x, and RISCV64. However, despite decades of development in compiler testing, testing Cranelift still presents unique challenges, including (1) constructing valid IR under the strict enforcement of SSA form, (2) generating sequences with sufficient computational density to stress backend components, and (3) balancing broad backend coverage with efficient root cause analysis across heterogeneous architectures.
  To address these challenges, we propose CLIR, a differential testing framework that integrates a syntax-preserving hierarchical generation strategy to guarantee SSA validity, a liveness-guided instruction refinement mechanism to maximize computational density, and a diagnosis-guided cross-architecture adaptation scheme to facilitate efficient root cause analysis across heterogeneous backends. Our comprehensive evaluation demonstrates that CLIR significantly outperforms existing state-of-the-art baselines, detecting 8x, 24x, and 8x more unique bugs than cranelift-fuzzgen, wasm-smith, and WASMaker, respectively, while RustSmith uncovered no bugs. Consequently, within 72 hours of testing, CLIR discovered 24 bugs spanning all target architectures, with 21 confirmed and 9 fixed.

</details>


### [11] [To Run or Not to Run: Analyzing the Cost-Effectiveness of Code Execution in LLM-Based Program Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26978v1)
*Zhihao Lin,Junhua Zhu,Mingyi Zhou,Xin Wang,Zhensu Sun,Renyu Yang,David Lo,Li Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 对基于LLM的程序修复代理中的执行行为进行了实证研究，发现执行频繁但收益集中，限制执行对成功率影响很小且能大幅降低成本，因此执行应作为资源进行成本效益权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于LLM的程序修复代理普遍采用执行驱动的范式，但执行的高成本及其对代理的实际效果尚未被充分研究，因此需要系统性地评估执行行为的影响。

Method: 采用两阶段实证研究：第一阶段分析SWE-bench排行榜上的7,745个代理轨迹以表征执行行为；第二阶段在200个SWE-bench实例上使用三个代理（Claude Code、Codex、OpenCode）和四种执行范式，进行3,000次端到端修复尝试，比较性能和成本。

Result: （1）平均每个任务8.8次测试运行，执行频率因代理和模型而异（2-19次），后期执行成功率更高；（2）禁止执行与无限制之间的解决率差距仅1.25个百分点且不显著，但禁止执行显著节省令牌和挂钟成本；（3）执行收益集中而非均匀。

Conclusion: 当前代理不加区分地使用执行，在低收益实例上浪费成本；执行应被视为一种资源，需明确进行成本效益权衡，而非作为默认能力。

中文摘要：基于LLM的程序修复代理越来越多地建立在“生成-运行-修订”范式上，通过迭代执行测试来评估和改进补丁。这种基于执行的方法已成为最先进系统的标准实践。然而，执行可能耗时且昂贵，但其对这些代理的影响仍未得到充分探索。在本文中，我们对基于LLM的程序修复中的执行行为进行了两阶段实证研究。为了大规模表征执行行为，我们首先分析了来自SWE-bench排行榜提交的7,745个代理轨迹。其次，我们在四个执行范式下评估了涵盖200个SWE-bench实例和三个代理（Claude Code、Codex和开源OpenCode）的3,000次端到端修复尝试，从而能够对性能和成本进行细粒度比较。我们的分析揭示了三个关键观察：（1）代码执行被用于所有分析的代理和模型中，平均每个任务有8.8次测试运行。执行行为在不同代理和模型之间存在显著差异，频率范围为每个任务2到19次，且后期执行的成功率始终高于早期执行。（2）执行限制对修复成功影响很小：在使用SOTA模型的商业代理上，禁止执行与无限制之间的解决率差距仅为1.25个百分点且不显著，而禁止执行节省了大量令牌和挂钟成本。（3）执行收益集中而非均匀。这些模式表明，当前代理不加区分地应用执行，在收益甚微的实例上付出了成本。因此，执行应被视为一种具有明确成本效益权衡的资源，而非默认能力。

Original abstract: LLM-based agents for program repair are increasingly built on a "generate-run-revise" paradigm, iteratively executing tests to evaluate and refine patches. This execution-based approach has become standard practice in state-of-the-art systems. However, executions can be time-consuming and expensive, yet their impact on these agents remains underexplored. In this paper, we conduct a two-stage empirical study over execution behavior in LLM-based program repair. To characterize execution behavior at scale, we first analyze 7,745 agent traces from SWE-bench leaderboard submissions. Second, we evaluate 3,000 end-to-end repair attempts across 200 SWE-bench instances and three agents (Claude Code, Codex, and the open-source OpenCode) under four execution paradigms, which allows for a fine-grained comparison of performance and cost. Our analysis reveals three key observations: (1) Code execution is used across all agents and models analyzed, with an average of 8.8 test runs per task. Execution behavior varies substantially across agents and models, with frequency ranging from 2 to 19 per task, and late-stage executions consistently achieve higher success rates than early-stage ones. (2) Execution restrictions have little effect on repair success: on commercial agents with SOTA models the resolve-rate gap between Prohibited and Unrestricted is only 1.25 percentage points and not statistically significant, while Prohibited saves substantial token and wall-clock cost. (3) Execution benefit is concentrated rather than uniform. These patterns suggest that current agents apply execution indiscriminately, paying its cost on instances where it provides little benefit. Execution, therefore, should be treated as a resource with an explicit cost-benefit tradeoff, not a default capability.

</details>


### [12] [How Much Static Structure Do Code Agents Need? A Study of Deterministic Anchoring](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26979v2)
*Zhihao Lin,Mingyi Zhou,Yizhuo Yang,Li Li*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 轻量级静态结构注释作为确定性锚点，能显著提升LLM代码代理的导航稳定性和可复现性，代价是少量额外输入令牌。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代码代理依赖关键词搜索，忽略代码结构关系，导致导航随机且难以复现。

Method: 在Codex基线中系统地注入不同粒度的静态结构注释（调用图、继承等），评估对定位、轨迹和稳定性的影响。

Result: 锚定效果：Func@5提升2.2pp，轨迹缩短1.6轮；规模敏感性：最优粒度取决于仓库，密集语义收益递减；稳定性：链接跟随率提高，方差减半，Pass@1提升3.4pp，输入令牌增加约10%。

Conclusion: 建议中型项目用轻量级拓扑，大型项目修剪前向边，隐式依赖用密集标签。

中文摘要：基于LLM的代码代理通过关键词搜索浏览仓库，但忽略了定义软件实际工作方式的结构关系，如调用图、继承层次和配置依赖。这使得代理导航具有随机性，且难以在不同运行中复现。我们研究轻量级静态分析是否能为这些代理提供确定性锚点：以纯文本注释形式注入的稳定结构事实，约束概率探索并使导航更可预测。从强大的基线（OpenAI的Codex）开始，我们系统地注入不同粒度的结构注释，并测量它们对定位、轨迹行为和运行间稳定性的影响。我们的研究发现了所谓的确定性锚定效应：静态结构的帮助更多不是通过使代理“更聪明”，而是通过使其导航更有纪律和可复现。三个观察支持这一发现：(1) 锚定有效：轻量级调用/继承拓扑改善了函数级定位（Func@5提升+2.2个百分点）并缩短了轨迹（-1.6个交互轮次）；(2) 锚定对规模敏感：最佳粒度和方向性取决于仓库特征，更密集的语义显示出收益递减，而枢纽密集的项目受益于仅反向链接（暴露“谁调用我”而不含前向边）；(3) 锚定稳定化：标签将链接跟随率从0.15-0.18提高到0.21-0.24，大致将运行间方差减半，并在中型仓库上提高了单次运行可靠性（Pass@1 +3.4个百分点），代价是大约10%的额外输入令牌。这些观察提出了实用指南：中型项目默认使用轻量级拓扑，大型仓库中修剪前向边，对隐式依赖情况保留密集标签。

Original abstract: LLM-based code agents navigate repositories through keyword search but miss the structural relationships, such as call graphs, inheritance hierarchies, and configuration dependencies, that define how software actually works. This makes agent navigation stochastic and difficult to reproduce across runs. We investigate whether lightweight static analysis can provide deterministic anchors for these agents: stable structural facts injected as plain-text comments that constrain probabilistic exploration and make navigation more predictable. Starting from a strong baseline, Codex from OpenAI, we systematically inject varying granularities of structural annotations and measure their effects on localization, trajectory behavior, and run-to-run stability. Our study identifies what we call the deterministic anchoring effect: static structure helps less by making agents "smarter" and more by making their navigation disciplined and reproducible. Three observations support this finding: (1) Anchoring works: lightweight call/inheritance topology improves function-level localization (+2.2pp Func@5) and shortens trajectories (-1.6 interaction rounds); (2) Anchoring is scale-sensitive: the optimal granularity and directionality depend on repository characteristics, where denser semantics show diminishing returns and hub-heavy projects benefit from inverse-only links that expose "who-calls-me" without forward edges; (3) Anchoring stabilizes: tags raise link-following rate from 0.15-0.18 to 0.21-0.24, roughly halve run-to-run variance, and improve single-run reliability (Pass@1 +3.4 pp) on medium-scale repositories, at the cost of roughly 10% more input tokens. These observations suggest practical guidelines: default to lightweight topology on medium projects, prune forward edges in large repositories, and reserve dense tags for implicit-dependency cases.

</details>


### [13] [Cleaning Logs for Downstream Tasks (Registered Report)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27000v1)
*Zahra G. Yazdi,Van-Hoang Le,Nyyti Saarimäki,Donghwan Shin,Domenico Bianculli,Lionel Briand*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LogPurifier是一种基于消息模板依赖关系的任务无关日志清理方法，旨在通过去除无关消息提升下游任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 日志中大量冗余和无关信息会降低模型推理和异常检测等下游任务的性能，因此需要自动清理日志数据。

Method: 提出LogPurifier，利用日志消息模板间的依赖关系识别并删除自由站消息，该方法与下游任务无关。

Result: 计划通过受控实验评估LogPurifier对模型推理和异常检测任务的效果和效率提升。

Conclusion: LogPurifier有望通过清理日志数据提高下游分析任务的性能，减少干扰信息。

中文摘要：背景：软件系统在执行过程中生成日志，以记录关键事件和运行时信息，用于故障排除和监控。然而，在实际中，日志通常包含大量冗余和无关信息，这会对下游分析任务（如模型推理和异常检测）的性能产生负面影响。目标：本研究的目的是通过识别和删除自由站消息（即与感兴趣的执行行为无关且与捕获系统功能行为的消息交错的消息）来清理日志数据。方法：为了实现这一目标，我们提出了LogPurifier，一种基于日志消息模板间依赖关系的任务无关日志清理方法。本文提出了一个使用受控实验设计的实证评估计划，以评估LogPurifier对两个下游任务（模型推理和异常检测）的有效性和效率的影响。

Original abstract: Background: Software systems generate logs during execution to record critical events and runtime information for troubleshooting and monitoring. However, in practice, logs often contain significant amounts of redundant and irrelevant information, which can negatively impact the performance of downstream analysis tasks, such as model inference and anomaly detection. Objective: The objective of this study is to clean log data by identifying and removing free-standing messages -- messages that are not relevant to the execution behaviors of interest and are interleaved with messages capturing the system's functional behavior. Method: To address this objective, we propose LogPurifier, a task-agnostic log-cleaning approach based on dependency relationships between log message templates. The paper presents a plan for an empirical evaluation using a controlled experimental design to assess the impact of LogPurifier on the effectiveness and efficiency of two downstream tasks: model inference and anomaly detection.

### [14] [The Spec Growth Engine: Spec-Anchored, Code-Coupled, Drift-Enforced Architecture for AI-Assisted Software Development](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27045v1)
*Hartwig Grabowski*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出Spec Growth Engine轻量级框架，通过规范图、上下文组装、增长协议和漂移门解决AI编码代理的上下文爆炸和规范-代码漂移问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编码代理加速实现速度，但导致上下文爆炸和规范-代码漂移两种结构性故障模式，现有规范驱动方法无法充分解决。

Method: 提出Spec Growth Engine，包含机器可读规范图（契约/设计分离）、Spine上下文组装器（所有权路径限定）、垂直切片增长协议（最难优先）和漂移门（阻止合并）。

Result: 框架能够有效处理上下文爆炸和规范-代码漂移，没有重量级框架的开销。

Conclusion: 综合现有软件工程原则形成一个精简、代码耦合、机器强制的整体，轻量级且有效。

中文摘要：AI编码代理极大地加速了实现速度，但引入了现有规范驱动方法未能完全解决的两种结构性故障模式：（1）上下文爆炸——代理必须同时推理整个仓库，随着上下文窗口填满，输出质量下降；（2）无声的规范-代码漂移——代码演变，规范没有，差异变得不可见，直到修复成本高昂。我们提出了规范增长引擎，一个轻量级框架，通过以下方式解决这两种故障模式：机器可读的规范图，其节点带有明确的契约/设计分离；Spine上下文组装器，将代理上下文限定为所有权路径；垂直切片增长协议，强制首次最难顺序；以及漂移门，使规范-代码偏离成为阻塞合并条件。该设计将成熟的软件工程原则（Parnas信息隐藏、C4、ADR、Walking Skeleton、Reflexion Models、Fitness Functions）综合成一个精简、代码耦合、机器强制的整体——而没有像RUP或MDA这样的重量级框架的开销。

Original abstract: AI coding agents dramatically accelerate implementation speed but introduce two structural failure modes that existing spec-driven approaches do not fully solve: (1) context explosion -- the agent must reason over an entire repository at once, degrading output quality as the context window fills; and (2) silent spec-code drift -- code evolves, the specification does not, and the divergence becomes invisible until it is costly to repair.
  We present the Spec Growth Engine, a lightweight framework that addresses both failure modes through a machine-readable spec graph whose nodes carry explicit contract/design separation, a Spine context assembler that scopes agent context to an ownership path, a vertical-slice growth protocol that enforces hardest-first ordering, and a drift gate that makes spec-code divergence a blocking merge condition.
  The design synthesises well-established software engineering principles (Parnas information hiding, C4, ADRs, Walking Skeleton, Reflexion Models, Fitness Functions) into a lean, code-coupled, machine-enforced whole -- without the overhead of heavy-weight frameworks such as RUP or MDA.

</details>


### [15] [ATGBuilder: Feature-Assisted Graph Learning for Activity Transition Graph Construction with Seed Supervision](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27080v1)
*Chenhui Cui,Zixiang Xian,Danyu Li,Tao Li,Rubing Huang,Dave Towey,Shikai Guo,Jiakun Liu*

TL;DR: 提出ATGBuilder，利用LLM和辅助重建目标构建高质量活动转换图，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有静态或动态ATG构建方法存在不完整或不准确的问题，而学习型方法对布局和小部件信息利用不足。

Method: 使用LLM总结UI活动元数据为文本功能摘要，并将小部件触发信息作为边属性，通过辅助重建目标训练模型。

Result: 在多个基准测试中显著优于最先进方法，并改善了自动化GUI探索工具。

Conclusion: ATGBuilder通过特征辅助图学习有效提升了ATG构建的质量和实用性。

中文摘要：Android应用程序围绕活动组织，这些活动提供可视化的图形用户界面（GUI）容器，用于承载UI并处理用户交互事件。活动转换图（ATG）被广泛用于建模应用程序的GUI导航。然而，构建高质量的ATG具有挑战性：基于静态分析的ATG可能遗漏可接受的转换，并提取不可行的转换；而动态探索的ATG可能产生不完整的转换。最近基于学习的方法可以将ATG构建视为种子监督的链接预测任务。然而，活动布局和小部件触发信息在ATG构建中的使用仍然有限。我们提出了ATGBuilder，一种特征辅助的图学习方法，用于种子监督的ATG构建。ATGBuilder使用大型语言模型（LLM）将布局中的UI活动元数据总结为紧凑的文本功能摘要。ATGBuilder显式地将小部件触发信息建模到边属性中：然后在模型训练期间利用这些信息上的辅助小部件属性重建目标。ATGBuilder的性能在前言语料库的一系列消融实验中进行了评估，并在基准测试上使用手动检查的真实ATG进行了实验。多个基准测试的实验表明，ATGBuilder显著优于最先进的方法。我们通过更好的导航指导改进自动化GUI探索工具，进一步展示了其有效性。

Original abstract: Android applications are organized around activities that provide visual Graphical User Interface (GUI) containers that host the UI and handle user interaction events. Activity Transition Graphs (ATGs) have been widely used to model apps' GUI navigation. However, the construction of high-quality ATGs is challenging: ATGs based on static analysis may miss acceptable transitions and may extract infeasible ones; while dynamically explored ATGs can yield incomplete transitions. Recent learning-based approaches can treat ATG construction as a seed-supervised link-prediction task. However, the use of activity-layout and widget-trigger information for ATG construction remains limited. We propose ATGBuilder, a feature-assisted graph-learning approach for seed-supervised ATG construction. ATGBuilder uses a Large Language Model (LLM) to summarize UI activity metadata from layouts into compact textual functionality summaries. ATGBuilder explicitly models widget-trigger information into the edge attribute: It then uses an auxiliary widget-attribute reconstruction objective on this information during model training. ATGBuilder's performance was evaluated across a series of ablations on the frontmatter corpus, and an experiment on benchmark using manually-checked ground-truth ATGs. Experiments on multiple benchmarks show that ATGBuilder significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods. We further demonstrate its effectiveness by improving automated GUI exploration tools through better navigation guidance.

### [16] [On the Reproducibility of Quantum Software Defect Datasets: A Case Study of Bugs4Q](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27124v1)
*Haruto Ohto,Yuta Ishimoto,Shinsuke Matsumoto,Shinji Kusumoto*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究复制了先前关于经典软件缺陷数据集可复现性的工作，发现量子软件缺陷数据集Bugs4Q也存在类似问题，但修复方式需源代码修改而非仅调整版本，并提出了修补版本Bugs4Q-Robust。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作仅关注经典软件缺陷数据集，量子软件缺陷数据集的可复现性尚不清楚，因此本研究旨在验证这些发现是否适用于量子领域。

Method: 使用Bugs4Q数据集，在21个Qiskit库版本上执行77,700次量子程序运行，分析可复现性，手动检查根因，并基于观察创建修补版本Bugs4Q-Robust。

Result: Bugs4Q可复现性从62.2%下降到16.2%，93.6%失败与依赖相关，但大多数需源代码修改。Bugs4Q-Robust将可复现性提高到78.4%。

Conclusion: 量子软件缺陷数据集需要持续维护以适应快速演化的生态系统。

中文摘要：软件缺陷数据集的可复现性对于获得可靠且可比较的研究结果至关重要。Zhu等人已表明，诸如Defects4J之类的缺陷数据集自创建以来会随着时间推移出现复现失败（即报告的缺陷变得不可复现）。然而，尚不清楚这些发现是否适用于量子软件缺陷数据集。因此，我们使用Bugs4Q（一个广泛使用的量子程序真实缺陷数据集）对先前工作进行了重复性研究。我们的分析包括在21个核心库版本上的37个Bugs4Q工件进行的77,700次量子程序执行。实验结果表明，Bugs4Q的可复现性从Qiskit v0.20.1上的62.2%下降到v2.3.1（截至2026年4月1日的最新版本）上的16.2%。对根因的手动检查进一步表明，93.6%的失败与依赖相关。虽然这些发现与先前工作一致，但我们也观察到了差异。特别是，Bugs4Q中的大多数复现失败不能仅通过调整依赖版本解决，而是需要源代码修改，例如迁移导入路径和API调用。基于这一观察，我们整理了Bugs4Q-Robust，即Bugs4Q的修补版本，以恢复可复现性。Bugs4Q-Robust将Qiskit v2.3.1上的可复现性从16.2%提高到78.4%。我们的发现强调了在不断发展的量子软件生态系统中持续维护数据集的重要性。

Original abstract: The reproducibility of software defect datasets is essential for obtaining reliable and comparable research results. Zhu et al. have shown that defect datasets such as Defects4J suffer from reproduction failures (i.e., reported bugs become non-reproducible) as time passes since their creation. However, it remains unclear whether these findings generalize to quantum software defect datasets. We therefore conduct a replication study of the prior work using Bugs4Q, a widely used dataset of real-world bugs in quantum programs. Our analysis includes 77,700 quantum program executions of 37 Bugs4Q artifacts across 21 core-library versions. The experimental results showed that the reproducibility of Bugs4Q dropped from 62.2% on Qiskit v0.20.1 to 16.2% on v2.3.1, the latest version as of April 1, 2026. A manual inspection of the root causes further indicated that 93.6% of the failures were dependency-related. While these findings are consistent with those of the prior work, we also observed differences. In particular, most reproduction failures in Bugs4Q cannot be resolved merely by adjusting dependency versions; instead, they require source-code modifications such as migrating import paths and API invocations. Based on this observation, we curated Bugs4Q-Robust, a patched version of Bugs4Q to restore reproducibility. Bugs4Q-Robust increases reproducibility from 16.2% to 78.4% on Qiskit v2.3.1. Our findings highlight the importance of continuous dataset maintenance in the rapidly evolving quantum software ecosystem.

### [17] [Smaller Models, Unexpected Costs: Trade-offs in LLM Quantization for Automated Program Repair](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27205v2)
*Fernando Vallecillos-Ruiz,Giordano d'Aloisio,Max Hort,Luca Traini,Antinisca Di Marco,Leon Moonen*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: LLM量化在自动程序修复中能大幅减少内存占用，但会增加时间和能耗，且不同配置的权衡高度依赖模型架构和任务复杂度，没有一种普遍优越的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究仅用基准分数概括量化影响，忽略模型行为变化和非功能开销，需在复杂任务（如APR）中全面评估量化权衡。

Method: 在6个LLM上测试13种量化配置（不同位宽、方法、目标组件），使用APR基准（HumanEval-Java和Defects4J）进行实证评估。

Result: 量化模型修复的问题与基础模型重叠少，内存减少85%但推理时间和能耗增加，48%配置被帕累托支配。

Conclusion: 没有通用优越的量化方法，权衡取决于模型架构和任务复杂度，需针对具体场景选择配置。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）是强大的工具，并且越来越多地被用于复杂的软件工程任务。随着参数数量的增加，结果往往可以得到改善，但这也会带来大量的内存需求。虽然量化有效地减少了内存占用，但其整体影响通常仅通过基准测试分数来概括，这掩盖了模型行为的变化和非功能开销。在这项工作中，我们使用自动程序修复（APR）——一项复杂的软件工程任务——对LLM量化进行了实证评估。我们分析了涵盖不同位宽、方法和目标组件（权重和KV缓存）的13种量化配置，涉及六个具有代表性的LLM，并在两个APR基准测试（HumanEval-Java和Defects4J）上进行了评估。我们的发现表明，基础模型和量化模型可以提供不同的修复问题集，重叠很少，同时保持可比较的修复问题数量。尽管量化成功地将内存占用减少了高达85%，但它增加了推理时间和能耗，我们将其归因于次优的硬件利用率。我们的帕累托权衡分析显示，48%的被评估配置严格被替代方案支配。我们的发现并未确定一种优越的量化方法，而是强调了有效性、内存占用和能源效率之间的权衡对底层模型架构和任务复杂度的敏感性。

Original abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are powerful tools and have been increasingly adopted for complex software engineering tasks. As the number of parameters increases, results can often be improved, but this also imposes substantial memory requirements. While quantization effectively reduces the memory footprint, its overall impact is often summarized only by benchmark scores, which mask changes in model behavior and non-functional overheads. In this work, we conduct an empirical evaluation of LLM quantization using Automated Program Repair (APR), a complex task in software engineering. We analyze 13 quantization configurations spanning different bit-widths, methods, and target components (weights and KV-cache) across six representative LLMs, evaluated on two APR benchmarks (HumanEval-Java and Defects4J).
  Our findings reveal that base and quantized models can provide different sets of repaired problems with little overlap, while retaining a comparable number of repaired problems. Although quantization successfully reduces memory footprints by up to 85%, it increases both inference time and energy consumption, which we attribute to suboptimal hardware utilization. Our Pareto trade-off analysis shows that 48% of the configurations evaluated are strictly dominated by alternatives. Rather than identifying a superior quantization method, our findings highlight that the trade-offs between effectiveness, memory footprint, and energy efficiency are sensitive to the underlying model architecture and the complexity of the task.

### [18] [Beyond Objects](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27258v1)
*Daniel Jackson*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 放弃面向对象，采用解耦个体与模块的替代方法，以根本解决功能碎片化和混淆问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面向对象的核心原则导致功能碎片化和混淆，且后续发展未能解决根本问题。

Method: 提出放弃面向对象，采用将问题域个体与功能模块解耦的替代方法。

Result: 解耦方法能更自然地避免功能碎片化和混淆。

Conclusion: 面向对象原则是问题的根源，回归并采用解耦方法是更简单的解决路径。

中文摘要：面向对象的一个核心原则——即一个系统的功能可以在对应于问题域中个体的对象之间进行划分——已经影响了软件的规范、设计和实现超过五十年。后来的软件工程发展试图在这一原则的基础上进行构建。但实际上，这种划分既不自然也不直接，而这些后来发展试图缓解的问题——功能碎片化和混淆——实际上常常是这一基本原则的必然结果。因此，解决这些问题的一个更简单的途径是从头开始，放弃面向对象，并用一种替代方法取而代之，该方法将问题域中的个体与划分功能的模块解耦。

Original abstract: A core principle of object orientation -- that the functionality of a system can be partitioned amongst objects that correspond to individuals in the problem domain -- has influenced how software has been specified, designed and implemented for more than fifty years. Later developments in software engineering sought to build on this principle. But in fact this partitioning is neither natural nor straightforward, and the problems that these later developments sought to mitigate -- the fragmentation and conflation of functionality -- were often, in fact, the inevitable consequences of this founding principle. An easier path to addressing these problems therefore starts by going back, abandoning object orientation, and replacing it with an alternative approach that decouples the individuals of the problem domain from the modules that partition functionality.

</details>


### [19] [Speculative Refinement: A Hybrid Autoregressive Diffusion Decoding Strategy and Its Behavior Across Benchmarks](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27474v1)
*Aditi Gupta,Neel Mishra,Kushagra Trivedi,Pawan Kumar*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过推测性精炼（SpecRef）研究结合AR和扩散解码的生成系统评估，发现代码基准混淆结构发现与逻辑正确性、精炼张力现象、不同评估协议产生不同排名以及后处理问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 如何评估结合自回归（AR）和扩散解码的混合生成系统，并揭示现有评估协议的缺陷。

Method: 提出SpecRef，一种免训练混合方法，使用熵引导的选择性掩码从AR草稿热启动掩码扩散语言模型，并在六个基准上使用三种评估协议进行测试。

Result: 四项发现：（1）代码基准混淆结构发现与逻辑正确性；（2）多阶段校正存在精炼张力；（3）对数似然和生成评估排名不一致；（4）标准Python后处理破坏非AR生成器评估。

Conclusion: 这些观察适用于任何多阶段或非自回归生成管道，指向更具诊断性的评估实践。

中文摘要：我们应该如何评估结合自回归（AR）和扩散解码的生成系统？我们通过推测性精炼（SpecRef）来研究这个问题，这是一种免训练的混合方法，它使用熵引导的选择性掩码从AR草稿热启动掩码扩散语言模型。在六个基准（HumanEval、MBPP、GSM8K、BBH、ARC-Challenge、HellaSwag）上使用三种不同的评估协议（基于执行的pass@1、精确匹配、对数似然评分）评估SpecRef，我们发现了几个超出我们特定系统的相关发现：（1）代码基准混淆了结构发现与逻辑正确性：提供语法支架在不改变模型的情况下将准确率从接近零提升到20%以上，表明基线失败很大程度上是结构性的；（2）一种精炼张力现象，其中多阶段校正会破坏已经正确的标记，暴露出单一模型评估无法看到的基准饱和天花板；（3）对于同一模型对，对数似然和生成评估产生不同的模型排名，表明它们衡量不同的能力；（4）标准Python后处理会悄悄破坏非AR生成器的代码评估。这些观察适用于任何多阶段或非自回归生成管道，并指向更具诊断性的评估实践。

Original abstract: How should we evaluate generation systems that combine autoregressive (AR) and diffusion decoding? We study this question through Speculative Refinement (SpecRef), a training-free hybrid method that warm-starts a masked diffusion language model from an AR draft using entropy-guided selective masking. Evaluating SpecRef across six benchmarks (HumanEval, MBPP, GSM8K, BBH, ARC-Challenge, HellaSwag) with three distinct evaluation protocols (execution-based pass@1, exact-match, log-likelihood scoring), we surface several findings relevant beyond our specific system: (1) code benchmarks conflate structural discovery with logical correctness: providing a syntactic scaffold lifts accuracy from near zero to over 20% without changing the model, indicating that much of the baseline failure is structural; (2) a refinement tension phenomenon where multi-stage correction degrades already-correct tokens, exposing benchmark saturation ceilings invisible to single-model evaluation; (3) log-likelihood and generative evaluation produce different model rankings for the same model pair, suggesting they measure different capabilities; (4) standard Python post-processing silently breaks code evaluation for non-AR generators. These observations apply to any multi-stage or non-autoregressive generation pipeline and point toward more diagnostic evaluation practices.

</details>


### [20] [Contextual Associations Between Webpage Elements for Web Accessibility: An Empirical Study](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27506v1)
*Kishan Rakesh,Shiyi Wei*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本研究通过链接预测从可访问性树中恢复网页元素的上下文关联，并评估其跨网站泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 屏幕阅读器用户从元素列表导航时，常遇到孤立无意义的可访问名称（如“阅读更多”），而将其与上下文关联的机制缺失，且此前没有工作研究如何选择相关上下文元素。

Method: 构建35个网站的人工标注上下文关联数据集，将页面表示为可访问性树导出的图并增加DOM/CSS空间和语义特征，比较MLP、GCN、GAT、SEAL四种模型与两种启发式基线，采用留一网站交叉验证和Hit@K、MRR评估。

Result: 五个网站的试点研究中，四个学习模型的Hit@10在0.16-0.85之间，启发式基线在0.08-0.30之间；最终结果待完成。

Conclusion: 本研究贡献了网页上下文关联的人工标注数据集、链接预测在可访问性树图上用于上下文选择的实证评估以及跨网站泛化分析。

中文摘要：屏幕阅读器用户通过元素列表导航网页时，经常会遇到诸如“阅读更多”之类的可访问名称，这些名称根据W3C可访问名称和描述计算规范是有效的，但在孤立状态下无法解释。使这些名称有意义的周围元素存在于页面中，但没有任何机制将它们与目标元素关联。此前没有工作实证研究如何选择哪些周围元素与给定目标在上下文中相关。本注册报告研究是否可以使用链接预测从可访问性树中恢复人类感知的网页元素之间的上下文关联，以及学到的关联是否跨网站泛化。我们将构建一个包含35个网站上人工标注的上下文关联的数据集，这些网站按Tranco前百万列表分层，每个页面有三位独立标注者。每个页面表示为其可访问性树导出的图，并增加了来自DOM和CSS的空间和语义特征。我们比较了四种机器学习模型（MLP、GCN、GAT和SEAL）与两种启发式基线，采用留一网站交叉验证和预先注册的统计框架，使用Hit@K和MRR。我们已经进行了五个网站的作者标注试点研究，以建立流程和参数化功效模拟，四个学习模型的试点Hit@10在0.16到0.85之间，两个启发式基线在0.08到0.30之间。最终结果将在计划实验和分析完成后报告。本研究贡献了一个网页上上下文关联的人工标注数据集、一个在可访问性树图上用于上下文选择的链接预测的实证评估，以及一个跨网站泛化分析。

Original abstract: [Context] Screen reader users navigating webpages by element list often encounter accessible names such as "Read more" that are valid under the W3C Accessible Name and Description Computation specification but uninterpretable in isolation. The surrounding elements that would make these names meaningful exist in the page but are not linked to the target by any mechanism. No prior work has empirically studied how to select which surrounding elements are contextually relevant to a given target. [Objective] This registered report investigates whether human-perceived contextual associations between webpage elements can be recovered from the accessibility tree using link prediction, and whether the learned associations generalize across websites. [Method] We will construct a dataset of human-annotated contextual associations on 35 websites, stratified across the Tranco top-million list, with three independent annotators per page. Each page is represented as a graph derived from its accessibility tree, augmented with spatial and semantic features from the DOM and CSS. We compare four machine learning models (MLP, GCN, GAT, and SEAL) against two heuristic baselines under leave-one-site-out cross-validation with a pre-registered statistical framework, using Hit@K and MRR. [Results] We have conducted a five-site author-annotated pilot study to establish the pipelines and parameterize the power simulation, with pilot Hit@10 ranging from 0.16 to 0.85 across four learned models and 0.08 to 0.30 across two heuristic baselines. The final results will be reported after the planned experiments and analyses are completed. [Conclusion] The study contributes a human-annotated dataset of contextual associations on webpages, an empirical evaluation of link prediction for context selection on accessibility-tree graphs, and a cross-site generalization analysis.

</details>


### [21] [Test Case Selection for Deep Neural Networks: A Replication Study on LLMs for Code](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27601v1)
*Ali Asgari,Mitchell Olsthoorn,Annibale Panichella*

Main category: cs.SE

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模复制研究，评估了测试用例选择技术在LLM代码模型上的有效性，发现部分视觉DNN的结论可以泛化，但性能因任务和模型而异，不确定性特征适用于早期失效发现，表示特征适用于准确率估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前TCS技术研究几乎只关注视觉DNN，不清楚其发现是否适用于LLM代码模型，需要填补这一空白。

Method: 对17个微调模型实例、7个预测特征和13种选择策略（包括12种特征感知策略和SRS基线）在三个代码分类任务（克隆检测、漏洞检测、技术债务预测）上进行实证评估，从准确率估计和早期失效发现两个维度分析。

Result: 只有部分视觉DNN的结论泛化到LLM代码模型：不确定性特征对早期失效发现有效，表示特征对准确率估计更稳健，但性能因任务和模型而异，表明上下文依赖性。

Conclusion: TCS技术在代码LLM中的有效性是上下文相关的，研究为超越视觉DNN的可复制性提供了证据，并为运营评估提供了见解。

中文摘要：最近，测试用例选择（TCS）技术已被探索用于支持在有限测试预算下深度神经网络（DNNs）的运营评估，其中标注成本是主要关注点，尽早发现模型失效是关键目标。尽管先前的研究报告了有希望的结果，但现有的实证评估几乎完全集中于基于视觉的DNN和数据集，尚不清楚先前的发现是否泛化到LLM代码模型。本文对TCS技术在LLM代码模型背景下进行了大规模复制研究。我们重新审视了最初为DNN提出的既定TCS策略，并补充了之前未在TCS中评估的统计抽样策略。我们在三个与代码相关的分类任务上评估其有效性：克隆检测、漏洞检测和技术债务预测。该研究涵盖了17个特定任务微调模型实例、7个预测特征和13种选择策略，包括12种特征感知策略和简单随机抽样（SRS）作为特征无关基线。我们从两个维度评估性能：准确率估计和早期失效发现。结果表明，当TCS应用于代码LLM时，只有一部分针对基于视觉的DNN的报告发现可以泛化。特别是，基于不确定性的特征对于早期失效发现有效，而基于表示的特征对于准确率估计更稳健。同时，不同任务和模型之间的性能差异很大，表明TCS有效性依赖于上下文。总体而言，这项研究为TCS技术超越基于视觉的深度学习的可复制性提供了实证证据，并为其在代码LLM运营评估中的使用提供了见解。

Original abstract: Recently, test case selection (TCS) techniques have been explored to support the operational evaluation of deep neural networks (DNNs) under limited testing budgets, where labeling cost is a primary concern and uncovering model failures early is a key objective. Although prior studies report promising results, existing empirical evaluations focus almost exclusively on vision-based DNNs and datasets, leaving it unclear whether prior findings generalize to LLM code models. This paper presents a large-scale replication study of TCS techniques in the context of LLM code models. We re-examine established TCS strategies originally proposed for DNNs and complement them with statistical sampling strategies not previously evaluated for TCS. We assess their effectiveness on three code-related classification tasks: clone detection, vulnerability detection, and technical debt prediction. The study spans 17 task-specific fine-tuned model instances, 7 predictive features, and 13 selection strategies, including 12 feature-aware strategies and simple random sampling (SRS) as a feature-agnostic baseline. We evaluate performance along two dimensions: accuracy estimation and early failure discovery. The results indicate that only a subset of findings reported for vision-based DNNs generalize when TCS is applied to LLMs for code. In particular, uncertainty-based features are effective for early failure discovery, while representation-based features are more robust for accuracy estimation. At the same time, performance varies substantially across tasks and models, indicating that TCS effectiveness is context-dependent. Overall, this study provides empirical evidence on the replicability of TCS techniques beyond vision-based deep learning and offers insights into their use for the operational evaluation of LLMs for code.

</details>

### [22] [Clinical Harness for Governable Medical AI Skill Ecosystems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26494v2)
*Tianhan Xu,Lei Bao,Zhe Hu,Tian Shen,Yongxiang Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 定义临床AI技能，设计Clinical Harness运行时治理架构，包括注册、编排、约束、监控，并通过骨质疏松症案例展示知识驱动、数据驱动和物理增强技能的应用。

Result: 展示了如何通过治理架构支持生命周期护理，为未来医学智能体提供基础。

We define clinical AI skills and propose the Clinical Harness, a runtime governance architecture that registers, orchestrates, constrains and monitors them. Using osteoporosis as an exemplar, we show how knowledge-driven, data-driven and physics-enhanced skills can support lifecycle care and provide a governed substrate for future medical agents.

### [23] [Humans Disengage, Reasoning Models Persist: Separating Difficulty Registration from Deliberation Allocation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26502v1)
*Han-yu Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 分析推理模型在难题上的分配策略，对agent元推理可迁移。

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大型推理模型（LRMs）与人类在问题解决过程中，对于同一问题答错与答对时花费资源的模式相反：LRMs在答错时花费更多token，而人类则花费更少时间；这种差异只有在控制项目身份时才显现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究显示LRMs和人类在难题上花费更多时间，但未区分跨项目（难度注册）与项目内部（资源分配）模式，且人类与LRMs在项目内部的资源分配模式可能相反。本研究旨在分离这两个层面，验证这一假设。

Method: 使用公开的人类-LRM匹配语料库，对比人类和五种思考型LRM（以及非思考型基线）在难度注册（跨项目）和资源分配（项目内）上的表现，计算Cohen's d评估错vs对效应。

Result: 所有被试在跨项目上均显示难度注册（难度越高花费越多），但在项目内人类和LRMs模式相反：LRMs在答错时花费更多token（Cohen's d = 1.47-3.13），而人类在答错时花费更少时间。该分离在固定项目效应、多数据集下稳健，且在非思考型基线中不存在。

Conclusion: 人类和LRMs采用不同的停止策略：人类在预期成功时投入、预期失败时放弃；LRMs则因不确定性而延长推理链，导致出错时花费更多。两种策略共享难度信号但控制相反，仅通过项目内比较可区分；资源理性元推理框架可解释这一分歧。

中文摘要：大型推理模型（LRMs）在难题上花费更长时间，这与人类类似。这种表面上的相似性掩盖了项目内部的相反模式。当LRM答错一个问题时，它会比答对同一问题时花费更多的token；而人类则相反，他们在答错的题目上花费的时间更少。我们区分了两个层面的思考：反应时间如何跨项目追踪难度（注册），以及在项目身份固定的情况下，智能体是在自己的失败还是成功上花费更多（分配）。在一个公开的人类-LRM匹配语料库上，人类和所有五个思考型LRM都再现了已知的跨项目一致性（注册），但在项目内部出现分歧（分配）：每个LRM都显示出较大的“错vs对”效应（H-ARC上Cohen's d = 1.47-3.13），而人类则显示相反的符号。这种比较停留在每个智能体自身的尺度内；我们从未将秒和token放在同一个轴上。这种分离在项目固定效应下成立，在数据集间可重复，并且在一个非思考型基线中不存在。我们将人类的模式解读为投入与放弃：人们在他们预期能解决的题目上坚持，而放弃其余题目。我们将LRM的模式解读为长度由不确定性驱动：当模型不确定时，推理链会增长，而这恰是其容易失败的时候。两种策略在难度上产生相同的跨项目相关性，因此它们看起来在先前工作使用的度量上是一致的；这种分歧只有在项目身份固定后才显现出来。在资源理性的元推理下，这种分裂存在于两种共享难度信号但实施相反控制的停止策略之间；推理链长度捕捉到了信号而忽略了控制。

Original abstract: Large reasoning models (LRMs) take longer on harder problems, just as humans do. This surface similarity hides an opposite pattern within items. When an LRM gets a problem wrong, it spends more tokens than when it gets the same problem right; humans do the reverse, spending less time on the trials they get wrong. We separate two levels of deliberation: how response time tracks difficulty across items (registration), and, with item identity held fixed, whether an agent spends more on its own failures or successes (allocation). On a public matched human-LRM corpus, humans and all five thinking LRMs reproduce the known cross-item alignment (registration) but diverge within items (allocation): every LRM shows a large wrong-vs-right effect (Cohen's d = 1.47-3.13 on H-ARC) while humans show the opposite sign. The comparison stays inside each agent's own scale; we never put seconds and tokens on one axis. The dissociation holds under item fixed effects, replicates across datasets, and is absent in a non-thinking baseline. We read the human pattern as engagement versus abandonment: people stay on items they expect to solve and give up on the rest. We read the LRM pattern as length driven by uncertainty: chains grow when the model is unsure, which is exactly when it tends to fail. Both policies produce the same cross-item correlation with difficulty, so they look aligned on the measure prior work has used; the divergence shows up only once item identity is fixed. Under resource-rational metareasoning, the split is between two stopping policies that share a difficulty signal but implement opposite control; trace length captures the signal and misses the control.

</details>


### [24] [What the LLM Should Not Say: Boundary-Aware Context Grounding for A Seven-Channel EEG Agent](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26519v2)
*Zhiyuan Xu,Yueqing Dai,Junling Li,Junwen Luo*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出边界感知上下文基础，对agent grounding有参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出NeuraDock Agent，通过分离本地EEG数值引擎与LLM，实现硬件和实现感知的接地，防止无依据解释，并在数值重复性、故障注入和边界感知测试中验证机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通用LLM不自动知道传感器测量、算法实现和结论合理性，尤其在低通道EEG中易产生无依据解释。

Method: 提出NeuraDock Agent，开源架构，分离确定性本地EEG引擎与硬件感知语言层；引擎处理数值并生成允许列表摘要，LLM仅接收摘要和上下文包。

Result: 三个层面评估：1) 12个记录十次数值重复产生一致结果；2) 故障注入实验确认数据边界和人工制品保留；3) 边界感知基准测试36个问题在两种LLM和四种上下文消融下产生288个输出，支持硬件和实现感知接地。

Conclusion: 结果支持硬件和实现感知接地作为校准EEG代理接受、限定或拒绝的实用机制，但未建立临床有效性或验证的绝对认知负荷指数。

中文摘要：大语言模型（LLM）可以使科学软件更易使用。然而，通用模型不会自动知道特定传感器支持哪些测量、当前软件实现了哪些算法、或计算结果的哪些结论是合理的。这些区别对于低通道脑电图（EEG）尤其重要，因为稀疏的空间覆盖和可变的信号质量使得看似合理但无依据的解释容易产生。我们提出NeuraDock Agent，一种开源架构，将确定性本地EEG引擎与硬件感知语言层分离。数值引擎解析记录、执行质量控制、执行经过审查的频谱工作流，并写入机器可读的人工制品。LLM仅接收紧凑的、允许列表的摘要和版本化的上下文包。上下文描述七通道硬件、经过审查的工作流、结果字段、实现边界、科学限制和参考案例。原始EEG和密集的逐样本数组保留在本地。我们在三个层面评估系统。首先，12个记录在十次数值重复中产生相同的结构化结果，完整的静息/任务运行在三次重复中产生相同的结果、报告和图形哈希。其次，请求捕获和故障注入实验确认了测试数据边界以及在HTTP、畸形输出和连接故障下本地人工制品的保留。第三，边界感知基准测试测试了36个普通和对抗性问题，在四种上下文消融和两个LLM下，产生288个输出。这些结果支持硬件和实现感知的接地作为校准EEG代理接受、限定或拒绝的实用机制；它们并未建立临床有效性或经过验证的绝对认知负荷指数。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can make scientific software easier to use. However, a general model does not automatically know which measurements a particular sensor can support, which algorithms are implemented in the current software, or which conclusions are justified by a computed result. These distinctions are especially important for low-channel electroencephalography (EEG), where sparse spatial coverage and variable signal quality make plausible but unsupported interpretations easy to produce. We present NeuraDock Agent, an open-source architecture that separates a deterministic local EEG engine from a hardware-aware language layer. The numerical engine parses recordings, performs quality control, executes reviewed spectral workflows, and writes machine-readable artifacts. The LLM receives only a compact, allowlisted summary and a versioned context pack. The context describes the seven-channel hardware, reviewed workflows, result fields, implementation boundaries, scientific limits, and reference cases. Raw EEG and dense per-sample arrays remain local
  We evaluate the system at three levels. First, 12 recordings produced identical structured results over ten numerical repetitions, and a complete Rest/Task run produced identical result, report, and figure hashes over three repetitions. Second, request-capture and failure-injection experiments confirmed the tested data boundary and preservation of local artifacts under HTTP, malformed-output, and connection failures. Third, a boundary-awareness benchmark tested 36 ordinary and adversarial questions under four context ablations and two LLMs, yielding 288 outputs.These results support hardware- and implementation-aware grounding as a practical mechanism for calibrating what an EEG agent accepts, qualifies, or refuses; they do not establish clinical validity or a validated absolute cognitive-load index.

### [25] [EvoOptiGraph: Weakness-Driven Coevolution via Graph-Based Structural Generation for Optimization Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26578v1)
*Qingcan Kang,Mingyang Liu,Xiaojin Fu,Shixiong Kai,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出LLM与进化图操作共进化生成MILP实例，可用于优化建模自动化，与自动代码优化相关

TL;DR: 提出EvoOptiGraph框架，通过数据和模型共同进化，生成结构多样实例，提高LLM优化建模能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM从自然语言优化建模面临训练数据缺乏结构多样性和数据生成与模型学习脱节的问题。

Method: 提出EvoOptiGraph，将MILP表示为属性二分图，使用进化算子生成实例，通过确定性编译和回译转换，采用SFT+RLVR训练，利用弱点信号生成新实例，形成闭环。

Result: 在六个数据集上，EvoOptiGraph在准确性、可执行性和泛化方面显著优于其他方法。

Conclusion: 目标导向的数据-模型共同进化是提升LLM优化建模任务的有效策略。

中文摘要：使用大型语言模型（LLM）从自然语言自动化优化建模面临两个关键挑战。首先，训练语料库缺乏结构多样性。其次，数据生成流程仍然静态且与模型学习脱节。为了解决这些挑战，我们提出EvoOptiGraph，这是一个新颖的框架，其中数据和模型在模型弱点的驱动下共同进化。EvoOptiGraph将每个混合整数线性规划（MILP）表示为一个属性二分图，并应用保持有效性的进化算子来生成结构多样化的实例。进化后的图通过确定性编译和经过验证的回译转换为求解器代码和自然语言。训练分为两个阶段：在初始数据集上进行监督微调（SFT），然后进行具有可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR），其中从图派生的弱点信号指导生成针对模型失败的新实例。这形成了一个持续更新训练分布的闭环。在六个公共数据集上的实验结果表明，EvoOptiGraph在准确性、可执行性和泛化能力方面显著优于更大的通用模型、基于智能体的方法和专门的基线。这些结果证明，目标导向的数据-模型共同进化是提高LLM在优化建模任务上表现的有效策略。

Original abstract: Automating optimization modeling from natural language with large language models (LLMs) faces two key challenges. First, training corpora lack structural diversity. Second, data generation pipelines remain static and decoupled from model learning. To address these challenges, we propose EvoOptiGraph, a novel framework where data and model co-evolve, driven by model weaknesses. EvoOptiGraph represents each mixed-integer linear program (MILP) as an attributed bipartite graph and applies validity-preserving evolutionary operators to generate structurally diverse instances. The evolved graphs are converted into solver code and natural language via deterministic compilation and verified back-translation. Training proceeds in two stages: supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on an initial dataset, followed by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), where graph-derived weakness signals guide the generation of new instances targeting the model's failures. This forms a closed loop that continuously updates the training distribution. Empirical results on six public datasets show that EvoOptiGraph significantly outperforms larger generalist models, agentic methods, and specialized baselines in accuracy, executability, and generalization. These results demonstrate that targeted data-model coevolution is an effective strategy for improving LLMs on optimization modeling tasks.

Result: 框架提高了AI调度的可执行性和可靠性，减少了瞬态机会损失，增强了错误修复和阻断能力，尤其在复杂场景中。

中文摘要：随着人工智能逐渐引入望远镜调度，基于AI的决策在处理复杂多约束问题方面显示出优势。然而，其输出常常存在数据引用不一致、推理错误和不可执行的决策，限制了在高可靠性观测任务中的适用性。在这项工作中，我们提出了一个多层次验证和可追溯推理框架，在执行前对AI生成的决策进行系统化的可靠性验证，并实现推理过程的显式表示以支持可追溯决策。该框架整合了数据引用验证、逻辑一致性检查以及观测和仪器约束验证，以过滤和纠正无效决策。它还引入了原子推理单元及其依赖关系，将调度决策表示为一系列相互连接的推理步骤，支持错误定位和事后分析。实验表明，该框架提高了AI调度的可执行性和可靠性，并减少了瞬态机会的损失。特别是，反馈纠正和推理步骤的结构化验证增强了对错误决策的修复和阻断能力，尤其是在复杂场景中。与纯AI方法相比，框架增强的方法在保持灵活性的同时显著提高了可靠性和可执行性。这些结果展示了将AI应用于高可靠性天文观测调度的可行且可验证的途径。

Original abstract: With the gradual introduction of AI into telescope scheduling, AI-based decision-making has shown advantages in handling complex multi-constraint problems. However, its outputs often suffer from inconsistent data references, reasoning errors, and non-executable decisions, limiting applicability in high-reliability observational tasks. In this work, we propose a multi-level validation and traceable reasoning framework that performs systematic reliability verification of AI-generated decisions prior to execution, and enables explicit representation of the reasoning process to support traceable decision-making. The framework integrates data reference validation, logical consistency checks, and observational and instrumental constraint verification to filter and correct invalid decisions. It also introduces atomic reasoning units and their dependency relationships, representing scheduling decisions as a sequence of interconnected reasoning steps that support error localization and post hoc analysis. Experiments show that the framework improves executability and reliability of AI scheduling and reduces loss of transient opportunities. In particular, feedback correction and structured validation of reasoning steps enhance the ability to repair and block erroneous decisions, especially in complex scenarios. Compared with pure AI methods, the framework-enhanced approach maintains flexibility while substantially improving reliability and executability. These results demonstrate a feasible and verifiable pathway for applying AI to high-reliability astronomical observation scheduling.

We present an autoformalization pipeline that translates agent prompts, MCP tool descriptions, and natural language policy documents into formally verified policies using an LLM-based generator-critic loop. The resulting policies are written in the Cedar Policy Language. On the MedAgentBench benchmark, our autoformalized policies cover substantially more of the source natural-language specification than the hand-coded symbolic enforcement in prior work.

### [28] [SKILL-DISCO: Distilling and Compiling Agent Traces into Reusable Procedural Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26669v1)
*Zhongxin Guo,Danrui Qi,Hanwen Gu,Peng Cheng,Yongqiang Xiong*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 从agent轨迹蒸馏可复用技能，直接适用于coding agent经验复用。

TL;DR: SkillDisCo通过蒸馏和编译从成功轨迹中提取可重用的程序化技能，显著提升任务成功率并减少执行回合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法从零开始重复解决类似任务，导致推理浪费和长执行轨迹；工作流复用和技能归纳对适用场景和共享结构表示缺乏明确指导。

Method: 提出SkillDisCo框架，将程序化技能定义为可重用的参数化PFSM子图，通过蒸馏从成功轨迹中提取这些子图，并编译为可调用、可执行、可验证的技能。

Result: 在ALFWorld和WebArena上，SkillDisCo在多个基准和模型规模下提升了成功率并减少了智能体回合数。

Conclusion: 将共享经验表示为可重用的执行结构（如PFSM子图）能有效提升Agent的性能和效率。

中文摘要：智能体通常从零开始重复解决类似的任务实例，导致不必要的推理成本和较长的执行轨迹。先前的工作已经探索了工作流复用和可执行技能归纳，但仍不清楚哪些任务场景允许程序化技能，以及如何在成功轨迹中表示共享的程序化结构。我们在FSM定义的场景中研究这个问题，其中成功轨迹可以被视为未知转换图中的路径，并将程序化技能形式化为可重用的参数化控制流子图。基于这种观点，我们引入了SkillDisCo，一个蒸馏和编译框架，它从成功轨迹中蒸馏出可重用的PFSM子图，并将它们编译成可调用、可执行和可验证的程序化技能。在ALFWorld和WebArena上的实验表明，SkillDisCo在多个基准和模型规模上提高了成功率并减少了智能体回合数，证明了将共享经验表示为可重用的执行结构的好处。

Original abstract: Agents often repeatedly solve similar task instances from scratch, leading to unnecessary reasoning cost and long execution traces. Prior work has explored workflow reuse and executable skill induction, but it remains unclear which task scenarios admit procedural skills and how the shared procedural structure should be represented across successful traces. We study this problem in FSM-defined scenarios, where successful traces can be viewed as paths in an unknown transition graph, and formulate procedural skills as reusable parameterized control-flow subgraphs. Based on this view, we introduce SkillDisCo, a distillation-and-compilation framework that distills reusable PFSM subgraphs from successful traces and compiles them into callable, executable, and verifiable procedural skills. Experiments on ALFWorld and WebArena show that SkillDisCo improves success rates and reduces agent turns across benchmarks and model scales, demonstrating the benefits of representing shared experience as reusable execution structures.

### [29] [Do Safety Guardrails Need to Reason? LeanGuard: A Fast and Light Approach for Robust Moderation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26686v1)
*Dongbin Na*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 探讨安全护栏是否需要推理，对agent可靠性设计有参考价值。

TL;DR: 提出LeanGuard，证明安全护栏不需要链式思维推理，通过轻量级编码器实现与推理护栏相当的性能，且计算量减少约100倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有护栏使用CoT导致模型重且慢，不适合设备端部署，因此质疑安全护栏是否真的需要推理。

Method: 在同一语料上训练轻量级双向编码器（标签编码器）和推理护栏，然后仅移除推理部分，保持其他固定，进行受控比较。

Result: LeanGuard（395M参数）在多个公开基准上平均F1为82.90，与更大解码器的推理护栏相当，推理计算减少约100倍，且对标签噪声更鲁棒、召回率更高。

Conclusion: CoT并未提高护栏准确性，现有基准可能不够难，CoT必要性未证实，并开源代码和模型。

中文摘要：为了筛查提示或响应，最近的护栏方法在发布判决之前会生成一个思维链（CoT）。这种设计遵循了一个普遍信念，即逐步推理能改善决策。然而，CoT也使得护栏变得沉重且缓慢，因为模型在决策前必须生成许多token。这可能不符合护栏的实际部署方式。护栏有时不应沉重和缓慢，它经常在设备上运行，例如在具身机器人上。在本文中，我们提出一个问题：安全护栏是否真的需要推理？为了回答这个问题，我们在同一语料上训练了一个轻量级双向编码器和一个推理护栏，然后我们仅移除推理部分，同时保持其他所有部分不变。通过这种受控的相同基线比较，我们表明思维链并未提高审核准确性。我们将由此产生的护栏命名为LeanGuard。一个395M的仅标签编码器在公开基准上达到了平均F1为82.90 ± 0.26。它与基于更大解码器的推理护栏性能相当，同时仅需对最多512个token的输入进行一次前向传播。这大约减少了100倍的推理计算。我们进一步表明，这种仅标签编码器在训练标签噪声下保持鲁棒性，并且在严格假阳性率下比推理护栏保留了更多的召回率，因此更重的推理护栏也并非更稳健的选择。我们的发现表明，当前的护栏基准可能不够难，不足以奖励推理，并且CoT对于审核的必要性仍未得到证实。我们在https://github.com/ndb796/LeanGuard发布了所有源代码和模型，包括LeanGuard。

Original abstract: In order to screen a prompt or a response, the recent guardrail methods generate a chain-of-thought (CoT) before they issue a verdict. This design follows a common belief that step-by-step reasoning improves a decision. However, CoT also makes the guard heavy and slow, because the model must generate many tokens before it decides. This may not match how guardrails are actually deployed. A guardrail sometimes should not be heavy and slow, and it often runs on-device, for example on an embodied robot. In this paper, we pose a question whether a safety guardrail really needs to reason. To answer this question, we train a lightweight bidirectional encoder and a reasoning guard on the same corpus, and we then remove only the reasoning while we keep everything else fixed. With this controlled same-base comparison, we show that the chain does not improve moderation accuracy. We name the resulting guard LeanGuard. A 395M label-only encoder reaches an average F1 of 82.90 $\pm$ 0.26 over public benchmarks. It matches a reasoning guard that is built on a much larger decoder, while it uses only a single forward pass over an input of at most 512 tokens. This is about a ~100x reduction in inference compute. We further show that this label-only encoder stays robust under training-label noise and retains far more recall at a strict false-positive rate than the reasoning guard, so a heavier reasoning guard is not the more robust choice either. Our finding suggests that the current guardrail benchmarks may not be hard enough to reward reasoning, and that the necessity of CoT for moderation is still not proven. We release all source codes and models including LeanGuard at https://github.com/ndb796/LeanGuard.

</details>


### [30] [Socratic agents for autonomous scientific discovery in high-dimensional physical systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26722v1)
*Xianrui Zeng,Pengfei Liu,Yirui Zang,Yang Shen,Fei Yu,Chunlei Yu,Minghao Liu,Yang Du*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出AHOIS，一个嵌入苏格拉底式助产术的多智能体AI科学家，在真实光学平台上实现自主假设提出和验证，无需先验知识，性能优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI科学发现系统缺乏认知自主性，无法自主构建、挑战和修正物理解释，需要从工作流程自动化迈向真正的自主科学。

Method: 开发AHOIS多智能体系统，包含物理学批评智能体，通过因果提问、约束检查、反例生成和证伪标准制定进行苏格拉底式审问，并闭环实验验证。

Result: 在多模光纤平台上，系统自主发现随机干扰编码假设、自适应稀疏测量策略、诊断故障模式，并转化成像协议。编码测量有效秩56.9，MNIST准确率76.97%，Fashion-MNIST 83.17%。

Conclusion: 苏格拉底式审问提升了物理一致性、假设完整性、不确定性校准和实验计划有效性，为基于证据、自我纠正的自主发现开辟了道路。

中文摘要：科学发现的自动化已到达一个转折点。虽然人工智能系统现在可以操作仪器、优化参数和生成假设，但大多数系统仍然是程序性的：它们执行由人类设计者固定的工作流程。真正的自主科学需要认知自主性——即构建、挑战和根据证据修正物理解释的能力。在此，我们介绍AHOIS，一个多智能体人工智能科学家，它将苏格拉底式助产术嵌入闭环实验。一个物理学批评智能体通过因果提问、约束检查、反例生成和证伪标准制定来审问假设。我们在一个真实的多模光纤光学平台上评估AHOIS，这是一个具有复杂波变换、间接检测、环境漂移和多模态采集的高维系统。在没有预先编码方案、分类器或散斑模型的情况下，该系统自主提出并验证了一个随机干扰编码假设，发现了任务自适应的稀疏测量策略，诊断了不同的故障模式（编码不稳定性、荧光污染和探测器噪声），并将一个已发表的成像协议转化为在非原始配置上可执行的工作流程。发现的编码实现了16x16测量，有效秩为56.9，MNIST分类准确率为76.97%，Fashion-MNIST为83.17%。消融实验表明，苏格拉底式审问提高了物理一致性、假设完整性、不确定性校准和实验计划有效性。这些结果建立了从工作流程自动化到在复杂物理环境中基于证据的、自我纠正的自主发现的途径。

Original abstract: The automation of scientific discovery has reached an inflection point. While AI systems now operate instruments, optimize parameters and generate hypotheses, most remain procedural: they execute workflows fixed by human designers. True autonomous science demands epistemic autonomy--the capacity to construct, challenge and revise physical explanations in response to evidence. Here we introduce AHOIS, a multi-agent AI scientist that embeds Socratic midwifery into closed-loop experimentation. A physics-critic agent interrogates hypotheses through causal questioning, constraint checking, counterexample generation and falsification-criteria formulation. We evaluate AHOIS on a real multimode-fibre optical platform, a high-dimensional system with complex wave transformations, indirect detection, environmental drift and multi-modal acquisition. Without prior encoding schemes, classifiers or speckle models, the system autonomously proposed and validated a random-interference encoding hypothesis, discovered task-adaptive sparse-measurement strategies, diagnosed distinct failure modes (encoding instability, fluorescence contamination and detector noise) and translated a published imaging protocol into an executable workflow on a non-original configuration. The discovered encoding yielded 16x16 measurements with effective rank 56.9 and classification accuracies of 76.97% on MNIST and 83.17% on Fashion-MNIST. Ablations show that Socratic interrogation improves physical consistency, hypothesis completeness, uncertainty calibration and experimental-plan validity. These results establish a route from workflow automation towards evidence-grounded, self-correcting autonomous discovery in complex physical environments.

### [31] [EGG: An Expert-Guided Agent Framework for Kernel Generation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26758v1)
*Yaochen Han,Ke Fan,Hongxu Jiang,Wanqi Xu,Weiyu Xie,Runhua Zhang,Chenhui Zhu,Yixiang Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 直接针对GPU kernel生成的agent框架，核心相关。

TL;DR: EGG是一个专家引导的代理框架，通过两阶段分解和阶段感知多代理协作，自动化生成高性能GPU内核，在KernelBench上实现2.13倍加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的内核生成方法缺乏领域特定优化指导，难以同时保证正确性和高性能。

Method: EGG将内核生成分解为算法结构设计和硬件特定调优两个层次阶段，并设计阶段感知的多代理协作机制。

Result: 在KernelBench和真实工作负载上，EGG相比PyTorch平均加速2.13倍，优于现有基于代理和基于RL的方法。

Conclusion: EGG通过专家引导和结构化分解有效提升了内核生成的性能。

中文摘要：高性能GPU内核对于降低大型语言模型（LLMs）指数级增长的计算成本至关重要，但其开发严重依赖领域专家的手动调优。虽然近期基于LLM的方法在自动化内核生成方面展现出潜力，但仍难以同时实现正确性和高性能。这一限制主要源于缺乏领域特定的优化指导，阻碍了优化空间的有效探索。我们提出EGG，一个专家引导的代理框架用于内核生成，该框架融入专家优化原则来指导LLM的决策。受专家工作流程启发，我们将内核生成分解为两个层次阶段：1）算法结构设计，建立高质量的计算结构基础；2）硬件特定调优，通过并行映射、张量分块和内存优化进行针对性调整。这种分阶段分解定义了明确的优化目标，结构化设计空间以实现逐步细化。为此，设计了一种阶段感知的多代理协作机制，用于阶段间和阶段内的上下文管理，确保稳定的优化轨迹。在KernelBench和实际工作负载上的实验表明，EGG相比PyTorch实现了2.13倍的平均加速，优于现有的基于代理和基于RL的方法。

Original abstract: High-performance GPU kernels are critical for reducing the exponentially growing computational costs of large language models (LLMs), but their development heavily relies on manual tuning by domain experts. While recent advances in LLM-based approaches show promise for automating kernel generation, they still struggle to achieve both correctness and high performance. This limitation primarily arises from the lack of domain-specific optimization guidance, hindering effective exploration of the optimization space. We propose EGG, an Expert-Guided Agent Framework for Kernel Generation, which incorporates expert optimization principles to guide LLMs' decisions. Inspired by expert workflows, we decompose kernel generation into two hierarchical stages: 1) algorithmic structure design, which establishes a high-quality computational structure foundation; 2) hardware-specific tuning, which performs targeted adjustments through parallel mapping, tensor tiling, and memory optimization. This staged decomposition defines explicit optimization objectives, structuring the design space to achieve progressive refinement. To this end, a stage-aware multi-agent collaboration mechanism is designed for inter and intra-stage context management, ensuring stable optimization trajectories. Experiments on KernelBench and real-world workloads show that EGG achieves a 2.13x average speedup over PyTorch, outperforming existing agent-based and RL-based approaches.

### [32] [Memory Depth, Not Memory Access: Selective Parametric Consolidation for Long-Running Language Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26806v1)
*Haoliang Han*

Main category: cs.AI

Selection reason: 提出记忆深度概念和选择性参数巩固机制，直接研究长程语言agent记忆策略，可迁移

TL;DR: 本文提出记忆深度问题，通过loop-drift协议和EVAF机制，证明选择性参数巩固与检索互补，并分解为选择与驱动两个维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长期语言代理需要持久的行为倾向，而现有检索系统无法决定哪些经验在上下文卸载后继续影响行为，因此需要研究记忆深度。

Method: 引入loop-drift协议作为压力测试，评估EVAF（惊喜-效价门控LoRA巩固）机制，并通过多种控制实验（随机门控、固定内循环、门控反转）分析选择性巩固的维度。

Result: 检索在浅层事实回忆上最优（准确率0.956-0.973），EVAF在目标持久性和卸载后恢复上更强（0.812-0.904），仅需少量参数写入；选择性巩固可分解为选择和驱动，且内循环写强度依赖模型，驱动校准时存在不对称耦合；陈旧记忆失效是未解问题。

Conclusion: 选择性参数巩固提供了与检索访问不同且互补的记忆深度，但陈旧记忆失效仍是边界挑战。

中文摘要：长期运行的语言代理不仅需要内存访问。检索系统可以在查询时获取过去的事实，但它们无法决定在工作上下文被卸载后，哪些经验应继续塑造行为。我们将这个独立问题研究为记忆深度：写入一个小型参数存储中的持久目标条件化倾向。我们引入了循环漂移协议（loop-drift protocol），一个受控的压力测试，其中检索索引保持完整，而工作上下文被卸载，目标条件化行为必须在长循环干扰下持续。我们评估了EVAF，一种基于惊喜和效价门控的LoRA巩固机制。在GPT-2和TinyLlama上，检索在浅层事实回忆方面最强（短事实准确率0.956-0.973），而EVAF在目标持久性和卸载后恢复方面最强（0.812-0.904），每200个事件仅进行2-3次参数写入。机制控制表明，选择性巩固可以分解为两个可控制维度：选择和驱动。匹配的随机门控将选择从稀疏写入中分离出来；跨GPT-2、TinyLlama和Mistral-7B的固定内部控制表明内循环写入强度依赖于模型；Mistral-7B的匹配门控反转揭示了在驱动校不准的情况下的不对称选择-驱动耦合。公共Memora事件流作为外部诊断，暴露了陈旧记忆失效作为一个未解决的边界。在这种探针中，选择性参数巩固提供了与检索访问不同且互补的记忆深度。

Original abstract: Long-running language agents need more than memory access. Retrieval systems can fetch past facts at query time, but they do not decide which experiences should continue to shape behavior after the working context is unloaded. We study this separate problem as memory depth: durable goal-conditioned tendencies written into a small parametric store. We introduce the loop-drift protocol, a controlled stress test in which the retrieval index remains intact while working context is unloaded and goal-conditioned behavior must persist under long-loop interference. We evaluate EVAF, a surprise- and valence-gated LoRA consolidation mechanism. Across GPT-2 and TinyLlama, retrieval is strongest on shallow factual recall (short-fact accuracy 0.956--0.973), while EVAF is strongest on goal persistence and post-unload recovery (0.812--0.904) with only 2--3 parametric writes per 200 events. Mechanism controls show that selective consolidation factorizes into two controllable dimensions: selection and actuation. Matched random gates isolate selection beyond sparse writing; fixed-inner controls across GPT-2, TinyLlama, and Mistral-7B show that inner-loop write strength is model-dependent; and a Mistral-7B matched-gate inversion reveals asymmetric selection-actuation coupling under miscalibrated actuation. Public Memora event streams serve as an external diagnostic, exposing stale-memory invalidation as an unresolved boundary. Within this probe, selective parametric consolidation supplies memory depth distinct from and complementary to retrieval access.
