### [63] [Risk-Aware Selective Multimodal Driver Monitoring with Driver-State World Modeling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26922v1)
*Daosheng Qiu,Haozhuang Chi,Hao Su,Shu Long,Xinyue Miao,Yongle Dong,Wei Zhang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 成本感知选择性推理框架用于驾驶员监控，选择性工具使用思想可迁移

TL;DR: 提出一种成本感知的选择性推理框架，结合轻量级RGB-生理学模型和学习门控，用于多模态驾驶员监测，实现了低延迟和低不安全假阴性率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型视觉-语言模型虽有多模态先验，但延迟和可靠性不适合实时驾驶员监测；现有方法难以平衡延迟和安全性。

Method: 构建轻量级RGB-生理学学生模型，结合学习门控进行选择性推理，并引入驾驶员状态世界建模模块预测未来误差和行动成本。

Result: RGB-生理学模型在驾驶员需求识别上达到0.7440 Macro-F1和0.9099平衡准确率，延迟3.08ms；选择性推理将不安全假阴性从17.37%降至约5%。

Conclusion: 可靠边缘驾驶员监测需要风险感知选择性控制和群体鲁棒校准，仅改进感知主干不够。

中文摘要：在自动化车辆中连续监测驾驶员要求低延迟推理，同时避免在不确定的驾驶员状态下做出不安全决策。大型视觉-语言模型提供了广泛的多模态先验知识，但其延迟和在此设置中有限的可靠性使其不适合作为始终在线的车载监测器。我们提出了一种成本感知的选择性推理框架，用于可部署的多模态驾驶员监测。核心系统是一个轻量级的RGB-生理学生模型，结合了车载视觉观察与窗口级HR/EDA信号，以及一个学习的门控机制，决定何时接受快速预测或放弃以进行安全干预。额外控制实验表明，学习到的分数包含超出场景先验的样本级信息，而精确的生理同步仍然是一个限制。为了纳入预测证据，我们进一步研究了一个紧凑的驾驶员状态世界建模模块，该模块展开潜在的驾驶员状态特征，并估计未来快速模型误差和反事实的系统级行动成本。在场景诱导的驾驶员需求识别任务上，RGB-生理学生模型相比仅RGB和仅生理学的基线有所改进，达到了0.7440的宏F1分数和0.9099的平衡准确率，参数量为11.39M，推理延迟为3.08ms。成本感知的选择性推理将不安全假阴性从全快速推理下的17.37%降低到各个种子下的大约5%，同时保持了部署级别的延迟。虽然驾驶员状态世界建模提供了有价值的预测信号，但最差群体评估凸显了持续的操作点校准漂移。最终，可靠的边缘驾驶员监测不仅需要推进感知主干网络，还需要风险感知的选择性控制和群体鲁棒的校准。

Original abstract: Continuous driver monitoring in automated vehicles requires low-latency inference while avoiding unsafe decisions under uncertain driver states. Large vision-language models provide broad multimodal priors, but their latency and limited reliability in this setting make them unsuitable as always-on in-cabin monitors. We propose a cost-aware selective inference framework for deployable multimodal driver monitoring. The core system is a lightweight RGB-physiological student that combines in-cabin visual observations with window-level HR/EDA signals, and a learned gate that decides when to accept the fast prediction or abstain for safety intervention. Additional controls show that the learned scores contain sample-level information beyond scenario priors, while exact physiological synchronization remains a limitation. To incorporate predictive evidence, we further study a compact driver-state world modeling module that rolls out latent driver-state features and estimates future fast-model errors and counterfactual system-level action costs. On scenario-induced driver-demand recognition, the RGB-physiological student improves over RGB-only and physiology-only baselines, reaching 0.7440 Macro-F1 and 0.9099 balanced accuracy with 11.39M parameters and 3.08ms inference latency. Cost-aware selective inference reduces unsafe false negatives from 17.37% under always-fast inference to approximately 5% across seeds, while maintaining deployment-level latency. While driver-state world modeling offers valuable predictive signals, worst-group evaluations highlight persistent operating-point calibration drift. Ultimately, reliable edge driver monitoring requires advancing not only perception backbones, but also risk-aware selective control and group-robust calibration.

</details>


### [64] [In-Context Model Predictive Generation: Open-Vocabulary Motion Synthesis from Language Models to Physics](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26981v1)
*Xiaomeng Fu,Junfan Lin,Yang Liu,Yaowei Wang,Guanbin Li,Liang Lin,Ziliang Chen*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 结合LLM规划与模型预测控制进行运动合成，其闭环比对反馈机制可迁移至coding agent的迭代优化。

TL;DR: 提出ICMPG框架，结合语言模型规划与物理反馈，通过闭环细化生成语义保真且物理合理的运动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法在语义保真度和物理真实性之间难以兼顾，LLM方法语义好但物理差，物理模型物理好但语义差。

Method: 提出ICMPG，包含CAMG模块（LLM规划生成候选）和MPG模块（物理模拟+语义对齐评估选择），闭环迭代优化。

Result: 在标准及零样本开放词汇设置下，比基线更物理合理、语义保真，泛化性强。

Conclusion: 框架融合语义和物理，灵活适配不同LLM，实现更可控的文本驱动运动合成。

中文摘要：从文本描述中合成人体运动对于沉浸式数字应用至关重要，然而现有方法在语义保真度和物理真实性之间面临持续的权衡。基于大语言模型（LLM）的方法可以解释多样的开放词汇指令并组合高级动作计划，但它们通常生成违反物理约束的运动。物理感知模型通过模拟或控制提高了真实性，但在语义复杂性、细粒度指令和新颖概念方面存在困难。为了解决这一差距，我们提出了上下文模型预测生成（ICMPG），一个将语言模型规划与推理时物理反馈相结合的框架。ICMPG将运动合成重新构建为类似模型预测控制（MPC）的过程，包含两个模块。上下文感知运动生成（CAMG）模块使用LLM作为规划器，分解文本命令并从运动令牌生成候选运动序列。模型预测生成（MPG）模块通过物理模拟和语义对齐评估这些候选，估计复合奖励，并选择最佳序列以指导后续生成步骤。与开环生成不同，这种闭环细化使ICMPG能够同时适应输入语义和模拟物理环境，无需特定任务的策略重训练。在标准零样本开放词汇设置中的大量实验表明，ICMPG能够稳健地泛化到多样化的命令，并在评估基准上生成比代表性基线更物理合理和语义保真的运动。该框架弥合了语义解释和物理模拟之间的鸿沟，同时保持灵活性以整合不同的LLM主干，实现了更多样化和可控的文本驱动运动合成。

Original abstract: Synthesizing human motion from textual descriptions is essential for immersive digital applications, yet existing methods face a persistent trade-off between semantic fidelity and physical realism. Large language model (LLM)-based approaches can interpret diverse open-vocabulary instructions and compose high-level action plans, but they often generate motions that violate physical constraints. Physics-aware models improve realism through simulation or control, but they struggle with semantic complexity, fine-grained instructions, and novel concepts. To address this gap, we propose In-Context Model Predictive Generation (ICMPG), a framework that integrates language-model planning with inference-time physical feedback. ICMPG reformulates motion synthesis as a Model Predictive Control (MPC)-like process with two modules. The Context-Aware Motion Generation (CAMG) module uses an LLM as a planner to decompose textual commands and generate candidate motion sequences from motion tokens. The Model Predictive Generation (MPG) module evaluates these candidates through physical simulation and semantic alignment, estimates a composite reward, and selects the best sequence to guide subsequent generation steps. Unlike open-loop generation, this closed-loop refinement enables ICMPG to adapt motions to both the input semantics and the simulated physical environment without task-specific policy retraining. Extensive experiments across standard and zero-shot open-vocabulary settings show that ICMPG generalizes robustly to diverse commands and produces motions that are more physically plausible and semantically faithful than representative baselines on the evaluated benchmarks. The framework bridges semantic interpretation and physical simulation while remaining flexible enough to incorporate different LLM backbones, enabling more versatile and controllable text-driven motion synthesis.

</details>


### [65] [Learning to Fold: prizewinning solution at LeHome Challenge 2026 (1st place online, 2nd offline)](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27163v1)
*Ilia Larchenko*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 机器人折叠VLA agent，包含自我价值预测、异步训练等，可启发LLM agent的自我评估与训练流程。

TL;DR: 该工作提出了一套用于双臂衣物折叠的强化学习系统，通过VLA策略自预测价值函数，结合多种工程优化，在仿真和真实世界竞赛中取得顶尖成绩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决双臂衣物折叠竞赛任务，挑战在于需要高效且鲁棒的策略，能够从仿真迁移到真实世界。

Method: 改进VLA策略，使其自身充当价值函数，预测成功、进度等；结合AWR和RECAP进行流匹配；采用通过HuggingFace Hub的异步分布式训练/推出；使用汤普森采样优化推理超参数；通过相机对齐、数据增强和DAgger式HIL收集实现仿真到现实迁移。

Result: 在LeHome Challenge 2026在线仿真轮次中获得第一（62支队伍），在真实世界决赛中获得第二。

中文摘要：我描述了我对LeHome Challenge 2026（一个ICRA 2026双臂衣物折叠竞赛）的解决方案。该系统在在线（仿真）轮次中从62支队伍中排名第一，并在真实世界决赛中排名第二。它通过一个强化学习循环改进了视觉-语言-动作（VLA）策略。该策略是其自身的价值函数：预测动作的同一网络也预测成功、进度和一些任务相关的未来量，这些预测驱动优势估计、实时失败检测和候选选择。该工作主要是重新组合现有的强化学习思想，并结合了工程和优化贡献，这些贡献可以作为一个整体配方或单独使用：用于流匹配VLA的AWR + RECAP组合；通过HuggingFace Hub的异步分布式训练/推出管线；通过汤普森采样进行推理时超参数优化；一个包含相机对齐工具、强数据增强和类似DAgger的人机循环数据收集的仿真到现实配方。

Original abstract: I describe my solution to the LeHome Challenge 2026, an ICRA 2026 competition on bimanual garment folding. The system placed 1st of 62 teams in the online (simulation) round and 2nd in the real-world final. It improves a vision-language-action (VLA) policy with a reinforcement-learning loop. The policy is its own value function: the same network that predicts actions also predicts success, progress, and a few task-relevant future quantities, and those predictions drive advantage estimation, live failure detection, and candidate selection. The work mostly recombines existing RL ideas with engineering and optimization contributions that can be used together as one recipe or individually: AWR + RECAP combined for flow-matching VLA; an asynchronous distributed training / rollout pipeline through HuggingFace Hub; inference-time hyperparameters optimization via Thompson sampling; a sim-to-real recipe with camera-alignment tooling, heavy augmentation and DAgger-like HIL data collection.

### [66] [Advancing Omnimodal Embodied Agents from Isolated Skills to Everyday Physical Autonomy](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27251v1)
*Junhao Shi,Zezheng Huai,Siyin Wang,Jia Chen,Yubang Wang,Zhaoye Fei,Hechang Chen,Jingjing Gong,Xipeng Qiu,Yu-Gang Jiang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出OmniAct具身agent框架，包含分层规划、记忆压缩与异步验证，通用agent架构可迁移。

TL;DR: OmniAct通过分层异步架构（规划、记忆、验证分离）实现持久化具身智能，在40个真实世界任务中显著提升成功率并降低上下文消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有系统将网络物理动作、上下文管理和故障恢复分离处理，导致持久化自主性不足，需要统一框架解决。

Method: 提出OmniAct框架，包含多模态语义规划器、自适应分层记忆（事件边界压缩）和异步视觉抢占引擎。

Result: 在40个真实世界长时任务中，OmniAct在所有复杂度级别提升端到端成功率，保持近线性令牌消耗，并提升中规模模型性能。

Conclusion: 分层异步架构是实现持久化具身智能的有效途径，无需依赖单一模型。

中文摘要：在非结构化环境中构建持久化具身智能体需要统一协调跨网络（API、物联网）和物理（操作、导航）领域的异构工具，并能够从长时间运行中不可避免地出现的物理故障中自主恢复。现有系统将这些视为分离的问题：基于VLM的规划器缺乏统一的网络-物理动作空间，智能体框架积累无界上下文导致时间连贯性下降，VLA策略执行开环操作而不检测自身故障。我们认为持久自主性不需要单一模型，而需要一种分层异步架构，明确分离规划、记忆和验证。为此，我们提出OmniAct，一个集成多模态语义规划器以实现跨统一动作空间的技能路由、具有事件边界驱动压缩的自适应分层记忆以实现亚线性上下文增长，以及在物理执行期间闭合语义环的异步视觉抢占引擎的框架。在两个机器人平台协调四个物联网设备的40个真实世界长时任务中，OmniAct在所有复杂度级别上实现了端到端成功的一致改进，在10万+累积交互令牌中保持近乎平坦的令牌消耗，并将中规模开源模型提升到专有级别性能。

Original abstract: Building persistent embodied agents in unstructured environments demands unified orchestration of heterogeneous tools spanning both cyber (APIs, IoT) and physical (manipulation, navigation) domains, coupled with autonomous recovery from physical failures that inevitably arise over extended operation. Existing systems treat these as separate problems: VLM-based planners lack a unified cyber-physical action space, agent frameworks accumulate unbounded context that degrades temporal coherence, and VLA policies execute open-loop without detecting their own failures. We argue that persistent autonomy requires not a monolithic model but a hierarchical asynchronous architecture with explicit separation of planning, memory, and verification. To this end, we present OmniAct, a framework integrating a multimodal semantic planner for skill routing across unified action spaces, an adaptive hierarchical memory with event-boundary-driven compression for sub-linear context growth, and an asynchronous visual preemption engine that closes the semantic loop during physical execution. Across 40 real-world long-horizon tasks on two robotic platforms coordinating four IoT devices, OmniAct achieves consistent improvements in end-to-end success across all complexity levels, maintains near-flat token consumption over under 100k+ accumulated interaction tokens, and elevates mid-scale open-weight models to proprietary-level performance.

</details>


### [67] [E-TTS: A New Embodied Test-Time Scaling Framework for Robotic Manipulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27268v1)
*Wen Ye,Peiyan Li,Tingyu Yuan,Yuan Xu,Xiangnan Wu,Chaoyang Zhao,Jing Liu,Nianfeng Liu,Yan Huang,Liang Wang*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出E-TTS测试时缩放框架，结合推理与行动缩放及历史感知迭代优化，适用于长程agent任务。

TL;DR: E-TTS通过历史感知迭代精化与视觉语言验证器，统一了具身任务中推理与动作的测试时缩放，显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作缺乏对推理缩放机制的研究，且历史信息利用不足，导致动作缩放效果受限。

Method: E-TTS采用模块化框架，包含历史缓冲区、推理与动作验证器，通过闭环迭代精化和成对推理-动作联合采样评分实现统一缩放。

Result: 在4个基准、6个环境、3种具身和4个基座模型上，仿真提升33.14%，真实场景提升26.62%，无需额外训练数据。

Conclusion: E-TTS是一种有效且通用的测试时缩放框架，能显著提升机器人操作的性能。

中文摘要：最近，一些工作初步尝试研究了具身任务中的测试时缩放。然而，两个主要挑战仍未解决：（1）推理可以有效提升策略性能，但其缩放机制很少被研究；（2）历史信息至关重要，因为具身任务本质上是长期序贯的，仅依赖当前观察进行动作缩放因缺乏历史上下文利用而不足。为应对这些挑战，我们提出E-TTS，一个模块化、即插即用的具身测试时缩放框架，通过基于历史感知的迭代精化与视觉语言验证器，统一了机器人操作中的推理与动作缩放。为支持联合推理-动作缩放，E-TTS以成对方式进行推理-动作联合采样与评分。为更好利用历史信息，E-TTS使用历史缓冲区存储历史上下文，随后由推理和动作验证器评估采样候选。与传统开环TTS方法不同，E-TTS在采样过程中引入反馈生成，形成闭环迭代精化机制，提升了推理效率和环境适应性。每个组件作为独立且可组合的模块运行，可根据任务需求灵活自适应配置。为评估框架优势，我们在4个不同基准、6个环境、3种具身形态和4种基础视觉-语言-动作模型上进行了实验。结果表明，无需额外专家数据收集或重训练，E-TTS持续提升性能，在仿真中提升高达33.14%，在真实场景中提升26.62%。

Original abstract: Recently, a few works have made early attempts to study test-time scaling for embodied tasks. However, two major challenges remain unsolved: (1) reasoning can effectively improve the performance of the policy, but its scaling mechanism has seldom been studied; (2) historical information is essential, as embodied tasks are inherently long-horizon and sequential, making sole reliance on current observations for action scaling inadequate due to the lack of historical context utilization. To address these challenges, we introduce E-TTS, a modular and plug-and-play Embodied Test-Time Scaling framework that unifies reasoning and action scaling for robotic manipulation via history-aware iterative refinement with vision-language verifiers. To support joint reasoning-action scaling, E-TTS performs reasoning-action joint sampling and scoring in a pairwise manner. To better utilize historical information, E-TTS uses a history buffer to store historical context, which is then used by reasoning and action verifiers to evaluate the sampled candidates. Unlike conventional open-loop TTS methods, E-TTS introduces feedback generation into the sampling process to form a closed-loop iterative refinement mechanism, enhancing both inference efficiency and environmental adaptability. Each component functions as an independent and composable module, allowing flexible and adaptive configuration depending on task requirements. To evaluate the advantages of our framework, we conduct experiments across 4 different benchmarks, 6 environments, 3 embodiments, and 4 base vision-language-action models. The experimental results demonstrate that, without requiring additional expert data collection or retraining, E-TTS consistently improves performance, achieving up to a 33.14% increase in simulation and 26.62% in real-world scenarios.

</details>

### [68] [Adaptive Evaluation of Out-of-Band Defenses Against Prompt Injection in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26479v1)
*Praneeth Narisetty,Shiva Nagendra Babu Kore,Uday Kumar Reddy Kattamanchi,Jayaram Kumarapu*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: LLM agent的提示注入防御与自适应评估，涉及agent安全控制。

TL;DR: 本文总结了近期针对LLM代理间接提示注入的带外防御策略，指出其验证方法的局限性，并通过独立复现Progent的自适应攻击实验证明该防御在弱模型上仍有效（成功率从25.8%降至4.2%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有带外防御仅在静态基准上验证，而先前的带内防御在自适应攻击下被大量攻破，因此需要评估这些防御在自适应攻击下的实际鲁棒性。

Method: 我们定义了自适应评估的威胁模型和协议，独立复现并扩展了Progent在AgentDojo上的实验，使用自托管的Qwen2.5-7B模型（单H200 GPU），并设计了手动自适应攻击进行测试。

Result: 三次实验平均显示Progent将攻击成功率从25.8%降至4.2%，自适应攻击成功率仅为2.6%，防御有效。

Conclusion: 结果与带外防御比带内检测更难攻击的假设一致，但基于弱模型和单一攻击模板，需通过更强攻击（如白盒GCG）进一步验证。

中文摘要：近期工作（2024至2026年）已汇聚于一种防御使用工具的LLM代理免受间接提示注入的策略：与其训练模型拒绝恶意指令，不如在模型外部通过确定性策略强制执行安全，以调解代理的行为。诸如CaMeL、FIDES、Progent、RTBAS和FORGE等系统通过能力、信息流标签和引用监视器实现了这一点，且多个系统报告其在AgentDojo基准测试上几乎消除了攻击。我们做出两个贡献。首先，我们将这些带外防御组织为经典完整性保护（Biba）、引用监视和最小权限的实例，从而对它们覆盖和不覆盖的内容进行结构化比较。其次，我们警告说，每一种防御都仅在静态基准（固定的注入尝试集合）上得到验证，而正是同样的方法论使得带内防御看起来很强，直到自适应的、针对防御的攻击以超过90%的成功率破坏了其中十二种；我们指定了自适应评估所需的威胁模型和协议。然后，我们独立复现并扩展了Progent自身的自适应攻击分析，在AgentDojo上使用一个在单个H200上自托管的开源权重代理（Qwen2.5-7B）运行该协议，这是作者未测试过的设置。三次运行的平均结果显示防御有效：Progent将平均攻击成功率大致降低了六倍（从25.8%降至4.2%），而手动设计的自适应攻击并未提高成功率（2.6%）。这是一个在弱模型上使用单个黑盒攻击模板的小规模数据点；更强的优化（白盒GCG）攻击仍然开放。该结果与以下假设一致，但并未确立：确定性的带外强制对于自适应攻击者而言比带内检测更难攻击。

Original abstract: Recent work (2024 to 2026) has converged on a strategy for defending tool-using LLM agents against indirect prompt injection: rather than training the model to refuse malicious instructions, enforce security outside the model with a deterministic policy that mediates the agent's actions. Systems such as CaMeL, FIDES, Progent, RTBAS, and FORGE realize this with capabilities, information-flow labels, and reference monitors, and several report near-elimination of attacks on the AgentDojo benchmark. We make two contributions. First, we organize these out-of-band defenses as instances of classical integrity protection (Biba), reference monitoring, and least privilege, yielding a structured comparison of what they do and do not cover. Second, we warn that every one of them is validated only on static benchmarks (a fixed set of injection attempts), the same methodology that made in-band defenses look strong until adaptive, defense-aware attacks broke twelve of them at over 90% success; we specify the threat model and protocol an adaptive evaluation requires. We then run that protocol as an independent reproduction and extension of Progent's own adaptive-attack analysis, on AgentDojo, with an open-weight agent (Qwen2.5-7B) self-hosted on a single H200, a setting its authors did not test. Averaged over three runs, the defense held: Progent cut mean attack success roughly sixfold (25.8% to 4.2%), and a hand-crafted adaptive attack did not raise it (2.6%). This is one small-scale data point on a weak model with a single black-box attack template; a stronger optimized (white-box GCG) attack remains open. The result is consistent with, but does not establish, the hypothesis that deterministic out-of-band enforcement is a harder target for an adaptive attacker than in-band detection.

</details>


### [69] [MIRROR: Novelty-Constrained Memory-Guided MCTS Red-Teaming for Agentic RAG](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26793v1)
*Inderjeet Singh,Andrés Murillo,Motoyoshi Sekiya,Yuki Unno,Junichi Suga*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 针对agentic RAG的红队框架，涉及安全与工具操纵。

TL;DR: 提出MIRROR，一个统一跨表面红队框架，通过记忆引导的蒙特卡洛树搜索和新颖性约束，在多模态代理RAG系统的四个攻击面上实现高攻击成功率和低变异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有红队方法针对特定攻击表面且常用已知模板，导致高重复率（文本投毒73-84%），缺乏统一框架处理多模态代理RAG系统扩展后的多种攻击面。

Method: MIRROR采用记忆引导的蒙特卡洛树搜索，在显式新颖性约束下基于检索上下文生成候选，并通过确定性新颖性门拒绝重复候选，使检索信息指导搜索而不复制提示。

Result: 在四个攻击面上，MIRROR在图像投毒上ASR达76%（基线52%），编排器攻击ASR达97%且查询成本减半，跨表面变异系数0.47；而基线如后缀优化在文本投毒ASR 79%但直接查询仅1%。

Conclusion: MIRROR作为统一跨表面框架有效克服了专门基线的表面局限性，实现了高且稳定的攻击性能，并发布了ART-SafeBench数据集以促进进一步研究。

中文摘要：多模态代理检索增强生成（RAG）系统将攻击面扩展到提示注入之外，包括文本投毒、图像注入、直接查询攻击以及编排器级别的工具操纵。现有的红队方法通常是特定于表面的，并且经常重复使用已知的攻击模板；在文本投毒基准测试中，我们测量到73-84%的完全重复。我们提出了MIRROR，一个统一的跨表面框架，它执行记忆引导的蒙特卡洛树搜索，同时在显式新颖性约束下根据检索到的上下文调节候选生成。一个确定性的新颖性门拒绝任何在归一化比较下匹配检索集的候选，允许检索信息指导搜索先验，而不启用提示复制。在针对多模态代理RAG目标的四个攻击表面上，MIRROR在图像投毒上达到了76%的攻击成功率（ASR），而基线为52%；在编排器攻击上以一半的查询成本达到了97%的ASR；并且具有最低的跨表面变异性（变异系数0.47）。相比之下，专门的基线在各表面之间崩溃：后缀优化在文本投毒上达到79%的ASR，但在直接查询上只有1%。我们发布了ART-SafeBench，包含41,815条包内记录和运行时适配器，四个表面总计41,991+条记录。

Original abstract: Multimodal agentic retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems expand the attack surface beyond prompt injection to include text poisoning, image injection, direct-query attacks, and orchestrator-level tool manipulation. Existing red-teaming approaches are typically surface-specific and often recycle known attack templates; on text-poisoning benchmarks we measure 73-84% exact duplication. We present MIRROR, a unified cross-surface framework that performs memory-guided Monte Carlo tree search while conditioning candidate generation on retrieved context under an explicit novelty constraint. A deterministic Novelty Gate rejects any candidate matching the retrieval set under normalized comparison, allowing retrieval to inform search priors without enabling prompt copying. Across four attack surfaces on a multimodal agentic RAG target, MIRROR attains 76% ASR on image poisoning compared with 52% for baselines, 97% ASR on orchestrator attacks at half the query cost, and the lowest cross-surface variance (coefficient of variation 0.47). In contrast, specialized baselines collapse across surfaces: suffix optimization reaches 79% ASR on text poisoning but 1% on direct queries. We release ART-SafeBench with 41,815 in-package records and runtime adapters yielding 41,991+ total records across four surfaces.

</details>


### [70] [Chai: Agentic Discovery of Cryptographic Misuse Vulnerabilities](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26933v1)
*Corban Villa,Sohee Kim,Austin Chu,Alon Shakevsky,Raluca Ada Popa*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 提出AI agent（Chai）用于发现加密误用漏洞，采用差分测试和图传播，属于软件安全agent，方法可迁移至代码优化agent的验证流程。

TL;DR: Chai是一个AI系统，通过重新设计差异测试，从库级别编录密码学误用漏洞并沿依赖图传播，发现了超过100个漏洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI漏洞发现对内存安全有效，但密码学误用缺乏类似插桩技术，需要新方法。

Method: 利用AI改进差异测试的精度，将库中差异转化为下游应用漏洞线索，在依赖图中传播。

Result: 在X.509、JWT、SAML库中发现超过100个漏洞，包括SSL库的关键漏洞。

Conclusion: Chai颠覆了AI漏洞发现范式，通过库级编录和传播实现高效漏洞发现。

中文摘要：人工智能辅助的漏洞发现已被证明对诸如内存安全等错误类型有效，其中插桩技术可以确认内存违规并有效过滤误报。然而，许多危险的漏洞类型，例如密码学误用，缺乏任何类似的插桩技术。在这项工作中，我们提出了Chai，一个基于人工智能的系统，通过自然产生的信号来发现和验证密码学误用漏洞。为了实现这一点，Chai重新思考了经典的差异测试技术，利用人工智能来1) 提高检测库中真实安全问题的精度，以及2) 将通常被忽视的差异重新用作下游应用程序中实际漏洞的线索。通过这样做，Chai颠覆了当前人工智能漏洞发现的范式：不是审计一个代码库以发现许多缺陷，而是在库级别上编录缺陷，并将其传播到密码学依赖图中，从而带来复合的效率提升。我们在X.509、JWT和SAML库上评估了Chai。Chai发现了一个以前未知的、存在于为数十亿设备提供动力的SSL库中的关键漏洞，以及一个主要网络浏览器背后的库和另一个主要Linux发行版中的安全漏洞。总的来说，这些技术发现了超过100个漏洞。

Original abstract: AI-assisted vulnerability discovery has proven effective for bug classes like memory safety, where instrumentation confirms memory violations and efficiently filters false positives. Many dangerous vulnerability classes, such as cryptographic misuse, however, lack any comparable instrumentation. In this work, we present Chai, an AI-based system that discovers and validates cryptographic misuse vulnerabilities through naturally occurring signals. To achieve this, Chai rethinks the classical technique of differential testing by leveraging AI to 1) improve precision for detecting real security issues in libraries, and 2) repurpose commonly overlooked discrepancies as leads for tangible vulnerabilities in downstream applications. In doing so, Chai inverts the prevailing paradigm of AI vulnerability discovery: instead of auditing one codebase for many flaws, it catalogs flaws at the library level and propagates them across a cryptographic dependency graph, delivering compounding efficiency gains. We evaluate Chai across X.509, JWT, and SAML libraries. Chai discovered a previously unknown critical vulnerability in an SSL library that powers billions of devices, along with security bugs in one library behind a major web browser and another in major Linux distributions. In total, these techniques surfaced over 100 vulnerabilities.

### [71] [ShareLock: A Stealthy Multi-Tool Threshold Poisoning Attack Against MCP](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27027v1)
*Liwei Liu,Tianzhu Han,Zijian Liu,Zishu Dong,Na Ruan*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究针对MCP的多工具投毒攻击，属于LLM agent安全，可迁移至coding agent的安全防护。

TL;DR: 提出ShareLock，一种利用Shamir阈值方案的多工具投毒框架，通过将恶意指令分散到多个工具描述中实现高隐蔽性和容错性，在主流LLM上攻击成功率超过90%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单工具投毒方案易被检测，缺乏对多工具协同投毒的系统分析，需要一种更隐蔽且鲁棒的攻击方法。

Method: 采用Shamir阈值方案将恶意指令分割为秘密共享，分散嵌入多个工具描述；通过服务器更新时的隐蔽触发器重建指令。

Result: 在多个LLM和MCP客户端上，攻击成功率超过90%，且基于工具描述的检测成功率显著低于现有单工具方案。

Conclusion: ShareLock实现了高隐蔽性和鲁棒性的多工具投毒，对LLM驱动的智能体系统构成严重威胁，需引起安全社区重视。

中文摘要：随着LLM驱动智能体的快速发展，模型上下文协议（MCP）作为一种连接LLM与外部工具的开放协议，已迅速成为现代智能体生态系统的基础。然而，MCP的广泛采用也引入了新的安全威胁，例如工具投毒攻击（TPA），该攻击利用LLM-服务器交互注入恶意提示。现有的投毒方案通常采用单一明文嵌入范式，无法抵御人工检查或自动化检测器。当前研究仍缺乏对多工具投毒的系统分析，其中多个工具可被协同利用以分散检测风险。本文提出了ShareLock，一种利用Shamir阈值方案实现多工具阈值投毒框架，具备卓越的隐蔽性和容错性。ShareLock将恶意指令作为看似无害的秘密共享分散到多个工具描述中，同时实现信息论保密性和针对适度审计的攻击鲁棒性。在服务器更新期间植入隐蔽重建触发器后，聚合的共享重构出隐藏指令，导致系统资产或私人数据的重大泄露。为评估ShareLock的现实威胁，我们构建了涵盖四个多工具场景的综合基准，并在两个不同MCP客户端的主流LLM上进行了广泛实验。结果表明，ShareLock在基于工具描述的检测方面显著优于现有单工具投毒策略，同时保持平均攻击成功率超过90%。

Original abstract: With the rapid evolution of LLM-driven agents, Model Context Protocol (MCP), an open protocol bridging LLMs with external tools, has quickly become foundational to modern agent ecosystems. However, the expanding adoption of MCP has also introduced novel security concerns such as Tool Poisoning Attack (TPA), which exploit LLM-server interactions to inject malicious prompts. Existing poisoning schemes typically adopt a monolithic plaintext embedding paradigm, which fails to withstand manual inspection or automated detectors. Current research still lacks a systematic analysis on multi-tool poisoning, where multiple tools can be exploited cooperatively to disperse detection risk. In this paper, we introduce ShareLock, a multi-tool threshold poisoning framework that utilizes Shamir's threshold scheme to ensure exceptional stealth and fault tolerance. ShareLock distributes the malicious instruction as benign-looking secret shares across multiple tool descriptions, achieving both information-theoretic secrecy and attack robustness against moderate auditing. After a covert reconstruction trigger is planted during server update, the aggregated shares reconstruct the hidden instruction, resulting in critical breaches of system assets or private data. To evaluate the realistic threat of ShareLock, we constructed a comprehensive benchmark encompassing four multi-tool scenarios and conducted extensive experiments across mainstream LLMs on two distinct MCP clients. Our results demonstrate that ShareLock significantly outperforms existing single-tool poisoning strategies in tool description-based detection while maintaining an average attack success rate exceeding 90%.

### [72] [Tool Use Enables Undetectable Steganography in Multi-Agent LLM Systems](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.28425v1)
*Jimmy Laurence Rippin,Simon C. Marshall,David Demitri Africa,Christian Schroeder de Witt*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究多agent系统中的工具使用与隐蔽通信，涉及agent安全与协调，属于通用agent风险问题

TL;DR: 本文实证表明，具备工具使用能力的AI智能体能实现无法检测的隐写通信，主要风险从算法复杂性转向智能体间的协调问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论证明复杂的隐写方案在信息论或计算上难以检测，但实际智能体能否实现这些方案尚不清楚。本文旨在探索当前智能体编码模型在现实工具使用条件下的隐写能力，并评估协调风险。

Method: 通过实验让具备代码执行和网络搜索能力的智能体构建隐写系统，并引入谢林点框架和协调度量分析智能体间的方案选择趋同程度。

Result: 智能体能生成无法检测的隐写系统并适应缺失要素；在广泛方案族上存在趋同，但严格的一次性协调有限；共享环境和重复交互显著增加协调风险。

Conclusion: 隐蔽通信的主要威胁从智能体能否实现复杂隐写转向能否协调一致，战略遏制假说获得实证支持，需关注共同人工制品和工具介导交互的风险。

中文摘要：日益自主的智能体AI系统带来了新的多智能体风险，例如通过隐蔽通信渠道进行秘密勾结。对此类勾结企图的自然防御是监控明文通信，但监控的有效性因日益复杂的模型隐写术而受到质疑；事实上，已经提出了一些理论上在信息论或计算上与善意的明文通信无法区分的方案。在本文中，我们证明这些方案的复杂性不再构成安全障碍，因为当赋予现实的工具使用能力（如代码执行或通过网络搜索访问研究论文）时，智能体编码模型已经可以产生无法检测的隐写系统。当关键要素缺失时，智能体也会适应，例如通过添加模型采样组件或实现相关的键控编码方案。然后，我们将智能体之间的默示隐写协调构建为一个谢林点问题，并引入了协调度量来估计两个智能体在没有明确事先协议的情况下选择兼容方案的可能性。我们的结果表明，AI智能体之间隐蔽通信的威胁模型发生了转变，主要障碍不再是前沿智能体是否能理解和实现复杂的隐写系统，而是协调：独立行动的智能体能否在兼容的方案、密钥和参数上达成一致。我们发现，在广泛的方案族上存在显著的趋同，但严格的单次协调有限，这表明共享人工制品、重复交互和工具介导的搜索是隐蔽通信风险最严重的情境。总体而言，我们的发现为最近的战略遏制假说提供了实证基础，该假说假定有能力的智能体可以构建能够逃过监控的隐蔽渠道。

Original abstract: Increasingly autonomous agentic AI systems pose novel multi-agent risks, such as secret collusion via covert communication channels. The natural defence to these collusion attempts is to monitor plain-text communication, but the efficacy of monitors has been called into doubt by increasingly sophisticated model steganography; indeed, some theoretical schemes have been proposed that are information-theoretically or computationally indistinguishable from good-faith plain-text communication. In this paper, we demonstrate that the complexity of these schemes is no longer a safety barrier, as agentic coding models can already produce undetectable stegosystems when given realistic tool usage, such as code execution or accessing research papers through web searches. Agents also adapt when key ingredients are missing, for example, by adding model-sampling components or implementing related keyed coding schemes. We then frame tacit steganographic coordination between agents as a Schelling-point problem and introduce coordination metrics for estimating when two agents are likely to select compatible schemes without explicit prior agreement. Our results suggest a shift in the threat model for covert communication between AI agents, where the main barrier is no longer whether frontier agents can understand and implement sophisticated stegosystems, but coordination: whether independently acting agents can converge on compatible schemes, keys, and parameters. We find substantial convergence on broad scheme families but limited strict one-shot coordination, suggesting that shared artefacts, repeated interaction, and tool-mediated search are the settings where covert communication risks are most acute. Overall, our findings provide empirical grounding for the recent strategic confinement hypothesis, which assumes that capable agents can construct covert channels that survive monitoring.

</details>


### [73] [On the Inseparability of Instructions and Data in Shared-Embedding Sequence Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27567v1)
*Dewank Pant,Shruti Lohani,Avijit Kumar*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 证明prompt injection的不可避免性，对agent安全防御有结构性启发

TL;DR: 证明在共享嵌入架构中，完美防御提示注入在数学上不可能，需要架构上的指令与数据通道分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提示注入是LLM应用的最大安全风险，但所有现有防御均被攻破，需探究根本原因。

Method: 形式化提示系统为提示动作模型，定义语义忠实控制（SFC），并通过三个数学证明证明其在共享管道中不可实现。

Result: SFC在共享管道中不可实现，由三个不可能性定理支撑，且该结果是结构性的，而非当前防御的缺陷。

Conclusion: 提示注入无法通过更好的管道内分类或对齐消除，需要架构上分离指令和数据通道，类似于冯·诺依曼架构中代码-数据混淆的解决方案。

中文摘要：提示注入是LLM集成应用的首要安全风险，然而迄今为止提出的每一项防御措施都已失效。我们证明这并非偶然：在缺乏强制控制-数据分离的共享嵌入架构中，完美的提示注入防御在数学上是不可能的。我们将提示系统形式化为提示动作模型，其输出包括控制权威动作：拒绝决策、工具授权、策略路由和内存写入。我们定义了语义忠实控制（SFC），即此类行为仅依赖于不可信输入的含义，而非其编码方式。然后我们通过三个结果证明SFC在共享管道中无法实现：来源恢复不可能性（共享表示使得可信与不可信内容在统计上不可分，受总变差距离约束）；控制路径暴露（不可信令牌通过决定输出的相同注意力价值聚合进入控制相关计算）；以及有限覆盖不变性差距（有限训练无法在无限语义等价类上证明不变性）。我们基于生产分词器和模型的测量对每个量进行了实证。

Original abstract: Prompt injection is the top security risk for LLM-integrated applications, yet every defense proposed so far has been broken. We prove this is not a coincidence: in shared-embedding architectures that lack enforced control-data separation, perfect prompt-injection prevention is mathematically impossible. We formalize prompted systems as Prompted Action Models whose outputs include control-authoritative actions: refusal decisions, tool authorization, policy routing, and memory writes. We define Semantic-Faithful Control (SFC), the property that such behavior depends only on the meaning of untrusted input, not on how it is encoded. We then prove SFC is unachievable within the shared pipeline, via three results: a provenance-recovery impossibility (shared representations make trusted and untrusted content statistically inseparable, bounded by total variation distance); control-path exposure (untrusted tokens enter control-relevant computation through the same attention value-aggregation that determines outputs); and a finite-coverage invariance gap (finite training cannot certify invariance over infinite semantic-equivalence classes). We ground each quantity in measurements on production tokenizers and models.
  The result is structural, not a gap in current defenses. It mirrors the code-data confusion in Von Neumann machines that gives rise to buffer overflows, a vulnerability class that took decades of layered defenses (DEP, Write-XOR-Execute, ASLR, stack canaries, and ultimately memory-safe languages) to contain, because no single mechanism sufficed. The implication is the same: prompt injection cannot be eliminated by better in-pipeline classification or alignment alone. It requires architectural separation of instruction and data channels. We identify the root cause and the class of solution it demands.

</details>

# cs.CV [[Back]](#toc)

### [74] [Perception, Verdict, and Evolution: Hindsight-Driven Self-Refining Forensics Agent for AI-Generated Image Detection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26552v1)
*Yangjun Wu,Keyu Yan,Yu Liu,Jingren Zhou,Fei Huang,Rong Zhang,Zhou Zhao,Fei Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 提出事后自我反思进化agent，可迁移至代码agent的自我改进。

TL;DR: 提出ForeAgent，一种基于多模态大语言模型和迭代自进化的AI生成图像检测框架，通过感知-判决架构和多视角线索融合，以及后见之明驱动的自我精炼策略，在多个基准上取得最先进性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度伪造检测方法对细粒度伪影不敏感，且依赖静态合成监督，导致灵活性和成本问题。

Method: 采用感知-判决架构聚合语义、空间和频域特征，利用MLLM判决；通过采样-反思-进化范式的后见之明驱动自我精炼策略，反思失败案例并生成高质量推理轨迹，经双专家门控过滤后微调模型。

Result: 在Chameleon基准上准确率82.18%（+16.41%），在AIGCDetect-Benchmark上平均准确率93.3%，推理比GPT-5更一致且因果依据更强。

Conclusion: ForeAgent通过自我进化的智能取证框架，显著提升了AI生成图像检测的性能和推理质量，为深度伪造检测提供了新范式。

中文摘要：生成式模型的快速发展对现有的深度伪造检测方法构成了重大挑战，尤其是在高度逼真的AI生成图像广泛传播的背景下。尽管多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在这一任务上展现出强大潜力，但现有方法存在两个关键局限：对细粒度取证伪影的敏感性不足，以及依赖来自前沿模型的静态合成监督，导致灵活性有限且成本高昂。为解决这些问题，我们提出ForeAgent，一种用于AI生成图像检测的具有迭代自进化能力的智能取证框架。首先，ForeAgent采用感知-判决（Perception-Verdict）架构，聚合跨语义、空间和频域特征的多视角线索，并利用MLLM作为判决模块融合这些信号以得出逻辑依据的判决。其次，为了实现持续自我改进，我们引入了一种基于后见之明的自我精炼策略，遵循采样-反思-进化（Sampling-Reflection-Evolution）范式。该智能体在训练实例上进行推理展开。以真实标签作为后见之明，它反思失败案例和低质量推理轨迹，以生成更高质量的推理轨迹。然后，这些合成样本通过一个双专家质量门控模块进行严格过滤。ForeAgent通过在自我筛选的高质量样本上微调不断进化。大量实验表明，ForeAgent在Chameleon基准上达到了最先进的性能，准确率为82.18%（较AIDE提升16.41%），并在AIGCDetect-Benchmark上跨16个生成器实现了93.3%的平均准确率。此外，外部评估显示，与GPT-5和GPT-5-mini相比，ForeAgent产生了更一致且具有因果依据的推理。

Original abstract: The rapid advancement of generative models presents a significant challenge to existing deepfake detection methods, particularly given the widespread dissemination of highly realistic AI-generated images. Although Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) show strong potential for this task, existing approaches suffer from two key limitations: insufficient sensitivity to fine-grained forensic artifacts and reliance on static synthetic supervision from frontier models, leading to limited flexibility and high-cost. To address these issues, we propose ForeAgent, an agentic forensics framework for AI-generated image detection with iterative self-evolution. First, ForeAgent adopts a Perception-Verdict architecture that aggregates multi-view cues spanning semantic, spatial, and frequency-domain features, and leverages an MLLM as a verdict module to fuse these signals for a logical-grounded verdict. Second, to enable continual self-improvement, we introduce a Hindsight-Driven Self-Refining strategy following a Sampling-Reflection-Evolution paradigm. The agent performs inference rollouts on training instances. Guided by ground-truth labels as hindsight, it reflects on failure cases and low-quality reasoning trajectories to regenerate higher-quality reasoning traces. These synthesized samples are then strictly filtered through a dual-expert quality gating module. ForeAgent continuously evolves via fine-tuning on self-curated high-quality samples. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ForeAgent achieves state-of-the-art performance on the Chameleon benchmark, reaching 82.18% accuracy (+16.41% over AIDE), and achieves 93.3% mean accuracy on AIGCDetect-Benchmark across 16 generators. In addition, external evaluation shows that ForeAgent produces more consistent and causally grounded reasoning compared to GPT-5 and GPT-5-mini.

</details>


### [75] [Confidence-Aware Tool Orchestration for Robust Video Understanding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26904v1)
*Yangfan He,Yujin Choi,Jaehong Yoon*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 视频理解框架集成工具使用和置信度，agentic编排可迁移

TL;DR: 提出Robust-TO框架，通过每帧信任度评估和证据加权，显著提升视频推理模型在扰动下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频推理模型盲目信任所有输入帧，导致在现实扰动下性能大幅下降且不自知。

Method: 提出Robust-TO，集成每帧信任度评估，使用统一证据接口组织感知工具，通过可靠性-相关性评分选择可信帧，并采用三层证据加权和置信度-成本GRPO奖励优化。

Result: 在八个任务上，干净输入准确率56.4%，超强基线10.6p；扰动下准确率54.3%，超强基线5.8p，且下降最小。

Conclusion: Robust-TO有效解决盲目信任问题，显著提升视频推理在现实扰动下的鲁棒性和准确率。

中文摘要：视频推理语言模型隐含地假设每个输入帧同样可靠。这导致我们称之为盲目信任问题：在运动模糊、眩光或遮挡等现实扰动下，前沿视频推理模型在真实世界具身基准测试中可能遭受15-30%的准确率下降，同时并未意识到其视觉证据已退化。为应对这一挑战，我们提出Robust-TO，一种主动式视频理解框架，将每帧的信任度明确地整合到推理的每个阶段。Robust-TO将异构的视觉感知工具组织在统一的证据接口下。每个工具接收来自原始问题的子查询和一组由可靠性-相关性评分选择的可信帧。它返回共享格式的证据：具体预测（例如，边界框、运动轨迹、识别文本或动作标签）、时间定位和校准的可靠性评分。在推理过程中，这些校准分数在三层综合过程（高/中/低）中指导证据权重，并定义置信度-成本GRPO奖励，同时优化正确性、证据可靠性和效率。在两个视频推理基准测试的八个任务上，Robust-TO在干净输入上达到56.4%的平均准确率，超过最强开源基线10.6个百分点，并优于Gemini-2.5-Pro（46.2%）。在五种现实损坏类型下，Robust-TO保持54.3%的平均准确率，比最强开源基线高5.8个百分点，同时在所有比较方法中表现出最小的干净到损坏准确率下降。

Original abstract: Video reasoning language models implicitly assume that every input frame is equally reliable. This leads to what we term the Blind Trust Problem: under realistic perturbations such as motion blur, glare, or occlusion, frontier video reasoning models can suffer 15-30%p accuracy drops on real-world embodied benchmarks, while remaining unaware that their visual evidence has been degraded. To address this challenge, we propose Robust-TO, an agentic video understanding framework that explicitly integrates per-frame trustworthiness into every stage of reasoning. Robust-TO organizes heterogeneous visual perception tools under a unified evidence interface. Each tool receives a sub-query derived from the original question and a set of trustworthy frames selected by the reliability-relevance score. It returns evidence in a shared format: a concrete prediction (e.g., a bounding box, motion trajectory, recognized text, or action label), temporal grounding, and a calibrated reliability score. During reasoning, these calibrated scores guide evidence weighting in a three-tier synthesis process (high/medium/low) and define a confidence-cost GRPO reward that jointly optimizes correctness, evidence reliability, and efficiency. On two video reasoning benchmarks spanning eight tasks, Robust-TO achieves 56.4% average accuracy on clean inputs, surpassing the strongest open-source baseline by 10.6%p and outperforming Gemini-2.5-Pro (46.2%). Under five realistic corruption types, Robust-TO maintains 54.3% average accuracy, 5.8%p above the strongest open-source baseline, while exhibiting the smallest clean-to-corrupted accuracy drop among all compared methods.

</details>


### [76] [DMV-Bench: Diagnosing Long-Horizon Multimodal Agents' Visual Memory with Incidental Cue Injection](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27499v1)
*Yujin Tang,Chenming Shang,Ruize Xu,Nikhil Singh*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: 多模态agent视觉记忆的交互式benchmark，提出双编码记忆架构，可用于agent评测与设计

TL;DR: 提出了首个多模态智能体视觉记忆基准DMV-Bench，并设计了基于双编码理论的DualMem架构，在视觉记忆任务上显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体记忆研究几乎完全集中于文本，缺乏对视觉记忆在交互环境中的评估，因此需要构建一个专门针对多模态智能体视觉记忆的基准和相应方法。

Method: 构建DMV-Bench基准，基于电子商务目录确保视觉线索唯一性；提出DualMem架构，并行维护视觉和言语编码，采用非对称双编码机制。

Result: 在DMV-Bench上，DualMem在多种链长度下超越字幕基线和三种现有系统，并在控制记忆库大小和编码位置偏差后仍保持优势。

Conclusion: 视觉记忆对多模态智能体至关重要，DualMem通过双编码有效利用视觉线索，为多模态智能体记忆提供了新方向。

中文摘要：关于智能体记忆的研究已经迅速成熟，但几乎完全集中在文本方面：很少有现有的基准测试在交互环境中询问智能体何时真正需要记住它所看到的而不是它能写下来的内容。我们推出了DMV-Bench（代码：https://github.com/yyyujintang/DMV-Bench），这是首个针对多模态智能体视觉记忆的交互式基准测试。DMV-Bench基于一个包含1000种产品变体的受控家居装饰电子商务目录构建，其中文本泄露契约将每个任务的判别信号仅保留在像素中。在一系列自主购物会话中，每个访问过的产品图像都携带一个独特的、预渲染的偶然线索，随后要求智能体回忆特定的被线索标记的产品并导航到其URL。受双编码理论启发，我们提出了DualMem，一种并行维护视觉和言语编码的记忆架构。在DMV-Bench上，DualMem在Gemini 2.5 Flash和Qwen2.5-VL-7B上均优于字幕基线和三种最近的多模态智能体记忆系统，在每个链长度J∈{5,10,15,50}上均领先，并且领先优势在控制了记忆库大小和编码位置偏差后仍然存在，同时采用非对称双编码机制，其中视觉通道端到端地承载线索，而言语通道扮演较小的查询-定位角色。

Original abstract: Research on agent memory has matured rapidly, but almost entirely on the text side: few existing benchmarks ask, in an interactive environment, when an agent genuinely needs to remember what it saw rather than what it could write down. We introduce DMV-Bench (Code: https://github.com/yyyujintang/DMV-Bench), the first interactive benchmark for multimodal-agent visual memory. DMV-Bench is built on a controlled home-furnishing e-commerce catalogue of 1,000 product variants in which a text-leakage contract keeps the discriminative signal of each task in the pixels alone. Across a chain of autonomous shopping sessions, every visited product image carries a unique, pre-rendered incidental cue, and the agent is later asked to recall a particular cued product and navigate to its URL. Inspired by dual-coding theory, we propose DualMem, a memory architecture that maintains a visual and a verbal code in parallel. On DMV-Bench, DualMem outperforms a caption baseline and three recent multimodal agent-memory systems at every chain length J in {5, 10, 15, 50} on both Gemini 2.5 Flash and Qwen2.5-VL-7B, with the lead surviving controls for memory-bank size and encoding-position bias, and an asymmetric dual-coding regime in which vision carries the cue end-to-end while the verbal channel plays a smaller query-grounding role.

</details>


### [77] [Dismantling Pathological Shortcuts: A Causal Framework for Faithful LVLM Decoding](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27596v1)
*Liu Yu,Can Chen,Ping Kuang,Zhikun Feng,Fan Zhou,Gillian Dobbie*

Main category: cs.CV

Selection reason: LVLM幻觉校正的推理时框架，对agent可靠性和解码策略有启发

TL;DR: Fox是一种无需训练的推理时框架，通过诊断和干预注意力头的结构错位来消除LVLM中的对象幻觉，性能超越SID 29.1%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LVLMs存在对象幻觉，且现有方法未考虑决策关键步骤中注意力头从视觉证据解耦的动态结构错位。

Method: 提出Fox框架，包括视觉注意力熵探针无监督定位风险中介、数值logit饱和因果干预切断捷径、冲突门控协作解码策略。

Result: Fox实现SOTA性能，相比SID提升29.1%，同时保持语言丰富性。

Conclusion: 通过诊断和干预注意力头的结构错位，Fox有效消除LVLM的对象幻觉，验证了动态结构错位假说。

中文摘要：大型视觉-语言模型（LVLMs）表现出复杂的推理能力，但仍容易产生对象幻觉。与主流的注意力强度假设不同，我们揭示了一种更深层次的动态结构错位：在决策关键步骤中，特定的注意力头作为风险中介，从视觉证据解耦并锁定语言先验，从而触发幻觉。这建立了一种绕过视觉基础的病理捷径。为了消除这一问题，我们提出了Fox（通过表达修正实现忠实性与观察流），一个无需训练的推理时框架。Fox使用视觉注意力熵探针无监督地定位风险中介，诊断结构错位。然后，我们通过数值logit饱和执行有针对性的因果干预，物理上切断捷径路径。最后，一种冲突门控协作解码策略协调干预的忠实性与观察的流畅性。大量实验表明，Fox达到了最先进的性能，在保持语言丰富性的同时，比SID高出29.1%。代码可在https://github.com/Cc2021start/Fox获取。

Original abstract: Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs) exhibit sophisticated reasoning but remain susceptible to object hallucination. Deviating from the prevailing attention intensity assumption, we reveal a deeper dynamic structural misalignment: hallucination is triggered at decision-critical steps where specific attention heads, acting as risky mediators, decouple from visual evidence to lock onto language priors. This establishes a pathological shortcut that bypasses visual grounding. To dismantle this, we propose Fox (Faithfulness and Observational-flow via eXpression-rectification), a training-free inference-time framework. Fox diagnoses structural misalignment using a visual attention entropy probe to localize risky mediators unsupervisedly. We then execute a targeted causal intervention via numerical logit saturation to physically sever the shortcut path. Finally, a conflict-gated cooperative decoding strategy reconciles interventional faithfulness with observational fluency. Extensive experiments demonstrate that Fox achieves SOTA performance, outperforming SID by 29.1% while preserving linguistic richness. Code is available at https://github.com/Cc2021start/Fox.

</details>

# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [78] [Temporal Validity in Retrieval Memory: Eliminating Stale-Fact Errors for AI Agents over Evolving Knowledge](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26511v1)
*Neeraj Yadav*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出带时间有效性的检索记忆，解决agent知识过时问题。

TL;DR: MemStrata通过在双时间账本中记录事实的取代关系来解决RAG在知识演化中的过时问题，无需LLM调用，在演化知识上达到高准确率并消除过时事实错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG无法处理知识随时间演化的问题，当事实变化时，检索结果同时包含新旧值且嵌入相似度接近，导致智能体难以区分，AUROC接近随机。

Method: MemStrata采用确定性（主体、关系、客体）取代规则，在双时间账本中淘汰过时值，无需相似度阈值或LLM调用。

Result: 在6个基准上，静态知识持平RAG，演化知识准确率0.95-1.00（vs RAG 0.20-0.47），过时事实错误率约0%（vs RAG 15-40%），检索延迟约2.1秒（vs LLM重排序16-18秒）。

Conclusion: MemStrata有效解决了知识演化中的过时问题，性能优越，并开源了评估工具。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）使智能体能够访问积累的知识，但缺乏时间模型。当一个事实发生变化时（例如函数重命名或API重构），RAG会检索到过时的和当前的值，且它们的嵌入相似度几乎相同。智能体要么弃权，要么提供已被取代的事实。我们表明这是一个结构性问题：在一个校准数据集上，余弦相似度区分矛盾事实与重复事实的AUROC为0.59（接近随机），因为矛盾事实在嵌入相似度上往往比改述的重复事实更接近原始事实。我们提出MemStrata，一种维护时间有效性的检索记忆。它像RAG一样存储事实，保持静态召回，但当某个事实的值被反驳时，一个确定性的（主体、关系、客体）取代规则会在双时间账本中淘汰过时的值——无需相似度阈值，也无需调用LLM。在本地使用7B模型进行的六个基准测试中，MemStrata在静态知识上与RAG持平，在演化知识上达到0.95-1.00的准确率（而RAG仅为0.20-0.47）。核心结果是过时事实错误率：当需要回答时，RAG提供已被取代的值的时间占比为15-40%，而MemStrata将其降至约0%，这是RAG无法避免的一类失败。MemStrata在检索延迟（约2.1秒）方面优于使用LLM重排序的基线（约16-18秒）。我们发布了相关的工具、数据集以及一种无标注的评估协议，用于知识演化情境下的记忆评估。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) gives agents access to accumulated knowledge, but has no model of time. When a fact changes (e.g., a function is renamed or API restructured), RAG retrieves both the stale and current value with near-identical embedding similarity. The agent then either abstains or serves the superseded fact. We show this is a structural problem: on a calibrated dataset, cosine similarity distinguishes a contradicted fact from a duplicated one with AUROC 0.59 (near chance), as contradictions are often more embedding-similar to the original than rephrased duplicates.
  We present MemStrata, a retrieval memory maintaining temporal validity. It stores facts like RAG, preserving static recall, but when a fact's value is contradicted, a deterministic (subject, relation, object) supersession rule retires the stale value in a bi-temporal ledger - with no similarity threshold and no LLM call. Across six benchmarks run locally with a 7B model, MemStrata ties RAG on static knowledge and reaches 0.95-1.00 accuracy on evolving knowledge (where RAG reaches 0.20-0.47). The central result is the stale-fact-error rate: when required to answer, RAG serves superseded values 15-40% of the time; MemStrata drives this to ~0%, a failure class RAG cannot avoid. MemStrata achieves this at retrieval latency (~2.1s) versus ~16-18s for LLM-reranking baselines. We release the harness, datasets, and a marker-free evaluation protocol for memory under knowledge evolution.

</details>


### [79] [The Inattentional Gap: Task-Conditioned Language and Vision Models Omit the Safety-Critical Signals They Can Otherwise Report](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26529v2)
*Kwan Soo Shin,In Seok Kang,Yunkyung Min,Judy Yang,Munho Lee*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 揭示任务条件化导致安全信号忽略，对agent注意力机制有启发。

TL;DR: 该研究发现，在狭窄任务指令下，AI模型会抑制报告同时存在的安全关键信号，形成“注意缺口”，导致基准安全性与实际安全性脱钩，但通过外部开放式批评者可以缓解这一问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI安全性评估仅关注模型能否检测指定危险，但实际事故常源于未指定的危险，因此需要研究模型在聚焦任务下对并发安全信号的报告行为。

Method: 在放射学、驾驶文本和胸部X光片任务中，比较模型在无约束、狭窄指令和排他性指令下的报告率；通过输出范围分析和外部批评者干预探究机制。

Result: 聚焦指令抑制报告率高达0.92，排他性指令完全消除报告；抑制现象普遍存在且与模型规模无关，但不同模型系列差异显著；外部开放式批评者能恢复所有遗漏报告。

Conclusion: 存在“注意缺口”导致基准安全评估不可靠，提出报告完整性评估作为安全关键部署的必要条件。

中文摘要：人工智能安全性的评估方式取决于模型能否可靠地检测出它被指示要发现的危险，然而事故往往源于没有人指定的危险。我们表明，将语言或视觉模型限定于一个狭窄任务会抑制它对同时存在但能报告的安全关键信号的报告，这是一种机器版的“不注意盲视”，其机制与人类不同。在放射学和驾驶文本场景以及胸部X光片视觉任务中，通常部署这些系统时所使用的聚焦指令将报告率抑制了高达0.92（相对于同一模型在无约束条件下），而明确的排他性指令在放射学中完全消除了报告。抑制现象出现在每个测试的模型中，不随规模增大而减弱，在推理模型中持续存在，并且在不同模型系列间的差异大于规模间的差异。我们将这种分离命名为“注意缺口”，并认为它使测量的基准安全性与实际安全性脱钩：一个系统可以针对评估指定的危险获得近乎完美的分数，同时对造成伤害的危险视而不见。通过探究机制，我们将近端触发因素定位于输出范围，并在采样系统中发现系统1式的任务捕获而缺乏可靠的内在监督。然而，监督可以从外部提供：将每个狭窄报告路由到一个独立的开放式批评者，恢复了所有遗漏的发现，表明这个缺口既可测量也可缓解。我们提出“报告完整性评估”，即在要求系统发现的内容之外，同时对其未能报告的内容进行评分，作为安全关键部署的必要条件。

Original abstract: AI safety is evaluated by how reliably a model detects the hazards it is told to find, yet accidents often arise from the hazard no one specified. We show that conditioning a language or vision model on a narrow task suppresses its reporting of co-present, safety-critical signals it can otherwise report, a machine analogue of human inattentional blindness, produced by a different mechanism. Across radiology and driving text scenarios and chest-radiograph vision tasks, the ordinary focused instructions under which such systems are deployed suppressed reporting by up to 0.92 in report rate relative to the same models when unconstrained, and an explicit exclusive instruction abolished reporting entirely in radiology. Suppression appeared in every model tested, did not diminish with scale, persisted in a reasoning model, and varied more by model family than by size. We name this dissociation the Inattentional Gap and argue that it decouples measured benchmark safety from real-world safety: a system can score near-perfectly on the hazards an evaluation specifies while remaining blind to those that cause harm. Probing the mechanism, we localize the proximal trigger to output scope and find System-1-style task capture without reliable intrinsic oversight in the sampled systems. Oversight could, however, be supplied externally: routing each narrow report to an independent open-ended critic restored every omitted finding, demonstrating that the gap is both measurable and mitigable. We propose reporting-complete evaluation, scoring what a system fails to report alongside what it is asked to find, as a requirement for safety-critical deployment.

</details>


### [80] [Auditing Framing-Sensitive Behavioral Instability in Large Language Models for Mental Health Interactions](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26982v1)
*Abla Bedoui,Ashley L. Greene,Mohammed Cherkaoui*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 评估LLM在心理健康对话中的行为稳定性，揭示了上下文框架对模型行为的影响，对agent可靠性评估有参考价值。

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了不同上下文框架如何影响大型语言模型在心理健康支持场景中的响应一致性，并发现框架相关变异在模型内部表示中可解码且可部分通过激活引导调节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知语义相似的担忧通过不同框架呈现可能引发不同模型响应，但关于框架变异如何在模型内部表示中体现的研究不足，需要评估其对AI系统一致性和可信度的影响。

Method: 使用受控匹配提示，覆盖多种上下文框架条件，在多个指令调优模型家族上进行实验，包括逐层探针分析和激活引导实验。

Result: 框架系统地改变了模型响应倾向；行为相关信息在Transformer各层均可解码，但强度因架构而异；保留框架探针始终高于随机水平；激活引导可部分调节下游行为。

Conclusion: 对上下文变异的鲁棒性应作为评估心理健康对话AI系统一致性和可信度的重要考量。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLMs）正越来越多地被整合到心理健康支持工具和其他心理敏感的对话应用中。在这种情况下，行为稳定性和一致性对于可信赖的人机交互至关重要。然而，语义相似的问题可以通过不同的上下文框架呈现，可能引发不同的模型响应。这种框架敏感性变异性可能挑战用户对系统行为的预期，并使AI可靠性的评估复杂化。虽然先前的研究主要从行为层面考察了这些影响，但关于框架相关变异如何在已对齐语言模型的内部表示中反映的知之甚少。在这项工作中，我们使用跨多个指令调优模型系列的受控匹配提示，涵盖多种上下文框架条件来研究这些影响。跨架构来看，框架系统地改变了解释性响应倾向。逐层探针分析表明，行为相关信息在整个Transformer深度中保持可解码性，但解码强度存在架构依赖性变异。此外，尽管有强烈的词汇基线，跨架构的保留框架探针始终高于随机水平。激活引导实验进一步表明，与框架相关的表征方向可以部分调节下游行为结果。最后，这些发现表明，对上下文变异的鲁棒性可能是评估部署在心理健康导向交互中的对话AI系统的一致性和可信度时的一个重要考虑因素。

Original abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly being integrated into mental health support tools and other psychologically sensitive conversational applications. In such settings, behavioral stability and consistency are important for trustworthy human-AI interaction. However, semantically similar concerns can be presented through different contextual framings, potentially eliciting different model responses. Such framing-sensitive variability may challenge user expectations regarding system behavior and complicate the assessment of AI reliability. While prior studies have primarily examined such effects at the behavioral level, less is known about how framing-related variation is reflected in the internal representations of aligned language models. In this work, we investigate these effects using controlled matched prompts spanning multiple contextual framing conditions across several instruction-tuned model families. Across architectures, framing systematically alters interpretive response tendencies. Layer-wise probing analyses show that behavior-associated information remains decodable throughout transformer depth, with architecture-dependent variation in decoding strength. Moreover, held-out framing probes remained consistently above chance across architectures despite strong lexical baselines. Activation steering experiments further suggest that framing-associated representational directions can partially modulate downstream behavioral outcomes. Finally, these findings indicate that robustness to contextual variation may represent an important consideration when evaluating the consistency and trustworthiness of conversational AI systems deployed in mental-health-oriented interactions.

### [81] [Bridging Talk and Thought: Understanding Dialogue Dynamics Across Collaborative Problem-Solving Contexts](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27233v1)
*Zhengyuan Liu,Stella Xin Yin,Min-Yen Kan,Nancy F. Chen*

Method: 提出了一个分层两层编码方案，集成认知与非认知问题解决以及元认知调节机制，并应用于九个不同领域的数据集进行验证。

Conclusion: 元认知调节是区分深层协作的关键，该框架有助于优化和评估人机及多智能体协作系统。

中文摘要：我们提出了一个用于分析协作解决问题情境中对话的概念框架，重点关注人机与多智能体协作的新兴动态。随着智能系统成为能够自主推理和战略合作的主动代理，理解协作解决问题过程中的对话交互对于优化和评估此类伙伴关系变得越来越重要。我们的框架通过一个集成了认知与非认知问题解决以及元认知调节机制的分层两层编码方案，解决了当前分析方法的关键局限性。我们展示了该框架在涵盖多个领域的九个数据集上的有效性和泛化能力，并提供了关于人类与代理如何协调其知识、技能和努力以解决复杂问题的见解，特别表明元认知调节可能是更深度协作的重要判别因素。

Original abstract: We present a conceptual framework for analyzing dialogue in collaborative problem-solving contexts, with an emphasis on the emerging dynamics of human-AI and multi-agent collaboration. As intelligent systems become active agents capable of autonomous reasoning and strategic cooperation, understanding the dialogic interaction during collaborative problem solving is increasingly important for optimizing and evaluating such partnerships. Our framework addresses key limitations in current analytical approaches through a hierarchical two-layer coding scheme that integrates cognitive and non-cognitive problem solving with metacognitive regulatory mechanisms. We demonstrate its effectiveness and generalizability across nine datasets spanning multiple domains, and provide insights into how humans and agents coordinate their knowledge, skills, and efforts to solve complex problems, showing in particular that metacognitive regulation can be an essential discriminator of deeper collaboration.

### [82] [Empowering GUI Agents via Autonomous Experience Exploration and Hindsight Experience Utilization for Task Planning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27330v1)
*Tianyi Men,Zhuoran Jin,Pengfei Cao,Yubo Chen,Kang Liu,Jun Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 提出PEEU方法，通过自主经验探索与后见经验利用提升GUI agent的任务规划，直接适用于coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出PEEU方法，通过自主探索环境获取经验并利用事后经验合成高层训练数据，提升小型多模态语言模型的规划与跨网站泛化能力，7B模型达到30.6%准确率，优于32B模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型开源多模态语言模型在规划能力和跨网站泛化方面存在不足，尽管它们在成本和隐私方面有优势。

Method: 提出规划经验探索与利用（PEEU）方法，包括自主探索环境发现经验和利用事后经验合成严格对齐的高层训练数据；同时提出任务分解层次分析框架（TDHAF）用于分析组合泛化。

Result: 7B模型在真实世界基准上达到30.6%准确率，优于Qwen2.5-VL-32B模型。

Conclusion: 构建事后高层任务并利用经验对于小型多模态语言模型的分布外规划能力至关重要。

中文摘要：多模态网页代理可以协助人类操作重复的图形用户界面任务，其中有效的任务规划对于将复杂任务分解为可执行动作至关重要。尽管小型开源MLLM在成本效率和隐私保护方面优于商业大型模型，但它们存在规划能力弱和跨网站泛化能力有限的问题。为了解决这些限制，我们引入了规划经验探索与利用（PEEU）方法，该方法自主探索环境以发现经验，并利用事后经验合成严格对齐的高层训练数据。为了定量分析驱动性能的泛化行为，我们提出了任务分解层次分析框架（TDHAF），系统研究跨三个任务粒度（低、中、高水平）的组合泛化。我们的分析表明，掌握低层级原子技能并不能保证高层级规划能力，而高层级任务训练能产生更强的分布外泛化。在真实世界基准上的实验证明了PEEU的卓越有效性：我们的7B模型达到了30.6%的准确率，优于更大的Qwen2.5-VL-32B模型。这些表明构建事后高层任务并利用经验对于小型MLLM的分布外规划能力至关重要。

Original abstract: Multimodal web agents can assist humans in operating repetitive GUI tasks, where effective task planning is essential for decomposing complex tasks into executable actions. While small open source MLLMs are cost efficient and privacy preserving compared with commercial large models, they suffer from weak planning and limited cross website generalization. To address these limitations, we introduce the planning experience exploration and utilization (PEEU) method, which autonomously explores environments to discover experiences and utilizes hindsight experience to synthesize strictly aligned, high level training data. To quantitatively analyze the generalization behaviors driving this performance, we propose the task decomposition hierarchical analysis framework (TDHAF) to systematically study compositional generalization across three task granularities: low, middle and high levels. Our analysis reveals that mastering low level atomic skills does not guarantee high level planning competence, while high level task training yields stronger OOD generalization. Experiments on real world benchmarks demonstrate PEEU's superior effectiveness: our 7B model achieves 30.6% accuracy, outperforming the much larger Qwen2.5-VL-32B model. These demonstrate constructing hindsight high level tasks and leveraging experiences is crucial for OOD planning abilities of small MLLMs.

### [83] [Supersede: Diagnosing and Training the Memory-Update Gap in LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27472v1)
*Vedant Patel*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 诊断并训练LLM agent的记忆更新失败（Supersede），直接针对agent长程任务中的事实货币性问题，与SemOpt所需可靠状态管理高度相关。

TL;DR: 本文发现LLM智能体在长时间交互中存在事实更新的“取代差距”，即无法正确使用当前事实而丢弃过时事实，即使先进模型也存在该问题，并证明该差距可通过强化学习训练缩小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在长期多轮交互中需要处理事实变化，但现有模型在记忆维护方面存在根本性缺陷，且不能被更强的模型弥补，需要专门训练。

Method: 通过LongMemEval知识更新子集进行测量，揭示瓶颈在于记忆维护；开发Supersede强化学习环境，以事实新鲜度作为奖励信号；使用GRPO对Qwen2.5-3B进行微调。

Result: 在LongMemEval上，完整上下文准确率92%，但替换为自维护记忆后降至77%；对话增长24倍时准确率从68%降至28%，增加记忆无改善；微调后准确率从9.0%提升至16.7%。

Conclusion: 本文证明事实取代差距是可训练的，并首次提供了可训练的环境和证据，表明通过强化学习可以缩小这一差距。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体在长时间、多轮会话交互中运行，其中事实会发生变化：用户搬家、价格更新、计划修订。正确行动要求使用事实的当前值并丢弃已被取代的值。我们在真实对话数据上分离出这种能力，并表明它是一个独特的、尚未解决的失败。在LongMemEval的知识更新子集上，将智能体的完整上下文替换为有边界的、自维护的记忆，即使在先进模型（gpt-5.4）上，准确率也会从92%下降到77%，这一差距具有统计显著性（配对McNemar检验p<0.005），并且在不同模型规模上持续存在，而完整上下文的准确率饱和在92%附近。因此瓶颈在于记忆维护，而非理解，并且不能被更强的模型所弥补。我们接着探究这是否仅仅是记忆容量不足，结果发现并非如此：随着对话长度增长24倍，准确率进一步下降（从68%降至28%），而为智能体按比例提供更多记忆并没有带来可检测的恢复（28% vs 28%，n=25）。失败与对话长度成比例，而非压缩比。我们发布了Supersede，一个开放的强化学习环境（基于verifiers/prime-rl栈），将这一测量转化为训练信号：智能体因基于当前值回答而获得奖励，因使用过时值而受到惩罚。最后，我们闭环验证了该差距是可训练的：在此环境中对小型开源模型（Qwen2.5-3B）进行GRPO微调，使其在真实未见对话上的保留准确率几乎翻倍（从9.0%到16.7%，单次运行），且检查点曲线单调递增，表明学习到的策略（而非训练框架）带来了提升。据我们所知，这是第一个可训练的环境，其奖励目标着眼于时间事实的新鲜度，也是第一个关于取代差距可以被训练缩小（而不仅仅是测量）的证据。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents operate over long, multi-session interactions in which facts change: a user moves, a price updates, a plan is revised. Acting correctly requires using the current value of a fact and discarding values that have been superseded. We isolate this ability on real conversational data and show that it is a distinct, unsolved failure. On the knowledge-update subset of LongMemEval, replacing an agent's full context with a bounded, self-maintained memory drops accuracy from 92% to 77% even on a frontier model (gpt-5.4), a gap that is statistically significant (paired McNemar p<0.005) and persists across model scale while full-context accuracy saturates near 92%. The bottleneck is therefore memory maintenance, not comprehension, and is not closed by a stronger model. We then ask whether this is merely an undersized memory, and find it is not: as the conversation grows 24x, accuracy falls further (from 68% to 28%), and granting the agent proportionally more memory yields no detectable recovery (28% to 28%, n=25). The failure scales with the length of the conversation, not the compression ratio. We release Supersede, an open reinforcement-learning environment (on the verifiers / prime-rl stack) that turns this measurement into a training signal: agents are rewarded for answering from the current value and penalized for stale ones. Finally, we close the loop and show the gap is trainable: GRPO fine-tuning a small open model (Qwen2.5-3B) on this environment nearly doubles its held-out supersession accuracy on real, unseen conversations (9.0% to 16.7%, a single run), along a monotonic checkpoint curve indicating the learned policy, not the harness, carries the gain. To our knowledge this is the first trainable environment whose reward targets temporal fact-currency, and the first evidence the supersession gap can be trained down, not only measured.

</details>

### [84] [Solarsystem: A Validated Lightweight Python Package for Planetary Positions and Solar-Lunar Event Calculations](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.27055v1)
*Ioannis Nasios*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 提出一个轻量级、无依赖的Python包solarsystem，用于计算行星位置和日月事件，精度与JPL DE440相当。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了提供无需外部星历数据的便携、高效天文计算工具。

Method: 使用解析模型计算行星和月球位置，包含可选岁差修正；坐标变换功能。

Result: 与DE440相比，行星经度平均偏差0.44角分，纬度0.16角分；日月事件时间差约几分钟；月球照度差异约0.2%。

Conclusion: solarsystem包准确且计算高效，适用于多种天文应用。

中文摘要：本文介绍了solarsystem，一个经过验证的轻量级、无依赖的Python包，用于行星位置和太阳-月球事件计算。该包提供了主要行星、选定矮行星、半人马座小行星Chiron和月球的日心及地心位置，以及日出、日落、月出、月落和月球照度计算。附加功能包括常用天文参考系之间的坐标变换。所实现的算法采用解析模型，避免了对外部星历数据集的依赖，从而提供了便携且计算高效的解决方案，适用于广泛的天文应用。包含一个可选的岁差修正模型，可根据用户需求在修正岁差的参考系或固定历元框架下进行计算。使用Skyfield框架作为参考，将solarsystem的数值性能与JPL DE440行星历进行了评估。跨多个天体和扩展时间间隔的验证实验表明，与参考历元相比吻合良好，平均行星经度和纬度偏差分别约为0.44和0.16角分。太阳和月球事件计算的额外验证显示，与参考解的时间差异仅为几分钟，而月球照度估计差异约为0.2%。该包可通过PyPI直接安装，源代码、文档、验证笔记本和示例工作流程均可在项目仓库https://github.com/IoannisNasios/solarsystem中公开获取。

Original abstract: This paper presents solarsystem, a validated lightweight and dependency-free Python package for planetary positions and solar-lunar event calculations. The package provides heliocentric and geocentric positions for the major planets, selected dwarf planets, the Centaur Chiron, and the Moon, together with sunrise, sunset, moonrise, moonset, and lunar illumination calculations. Additional functionality includes coordinate transformations between commonly used astronomical reference systems.
  The implemented algorithms employ analytical models that avoid reliance on external ephemeris datasets, resulting in a portable and computationally efficient solution suitable for a broad range of astronomical applications. An optional precession correction model is included, enabling calculations either in a precession-corrected reference frame or in a fixed epoch framework, depending on user requirements.
  The numerical performance of solarsystem was evaluated against the JPL DE440 planetary ephemerides using the Skyfield framework as a reference. Validation experiments spanning multiple bodies and extended temporal intervals demonstrate good agreement with the reference ephemerides, with mean planetary longitude and latitude deviations of approximately 0.44 and 0.16 arcminutes, respectively. Additional validation of solar and lunar event calculations yielded timing differences of only a few minutes relative to the reference solutions, while lunar illumination estimates differed by approximately 0.2%.
  The package can be installed directly through PyPI while the source code, documentation, validation notebooks and example workflows are publicly available through the project repository in https://github.com/IoannisNasios/solarsystem.

</details>


<div id='cs.HC'></div>

# cs.HC [[Back]](#toc)

### [85] [HiLSVA: Design and Evaluation of a Human-in-the-Loop Agentic System for Scientific Visualization](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.26614v1)
*Kuangshi Ai,Patrick Phuoc Do,Chaoli Wang*

Main category: cs.HC

Selection reason: 提出plan-first多agent架构与人类监督，对设计coding agent有参考价值

TL;DR: HiLSVA通过人在环中的混合主动多智能体架构，在科学可视化中实现透明、可控且可溯源的协作分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体驱动的科学可视化系统过于强调自主性，缺乏透明度和人类监督，限制了人类对分析过程的控制。

Method: 提出HiLSVA系统，采用计划优先的多智能体架构，集成显式人类监督、逐步溯源追踪和测试时学习自适应，支持自然语言与直接操作交互，并通过沙盒环境确保安全与可复现性。

Result: 案例研究和12名用户实验表明，混合主动交互在不同专家水平下均提升了任务完成度、用户控制和工作流透明度，但存在执行效率与人类监督之间的权衡。

Conclusion: 强调了以人为中心的智能体设计在科学可视化中的关键作用，为未来协作可视化系统提供了指导。

中文摘要：大型语言模型（LLM）智能体能够实现科学可视化（SciVis）的自然语言交互。然而，先前的系统基本上优先考虑自主性而非人类分析控制，从而限制了透明度和人类监督。我们提出了HiLSVA，一个人在环中的智能体系统，支持混合主动的SciVis工作流程。HiLSVA集成了计划优先的多智能体架构，具有明确的人类监督、逐步溯源追踪以及基于用户反馈的测试时学习自适应。该系统通过自然语言和对可视化的直接操作支持人类与智能体之间的流畅切换，而沙盒执行确保安全、可复现的工作流程。通过这种方式，HiLSVA将智能体驱动的SciVis重新定义为增强而非替代人类分析推理的协作过程。我们通过代表性案例研究和一项受控用户研究（十二名不同专业知识的参与者，在多种自主性设置下）评估了HiLSVA。结果表明，混合主动交互提高了不同用户专业水平下的任务完成度、用户控制和工作流透明度，同时揭示了执行效率与人类监督之间的权衡。这些发现强调了以人为中心的设计在智能体驱动的SciVis中的重要性，并指导未来协作可视化系统的开发。我们鼓励读者访问https://hilsva.github.io/探索我们的演示视频、案例研究和源代码。

Original abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents enable natural language interaction for scientific visualization (SciVis). Still, prior systems have essentially prioritized autonomy over human analytical control, thereby limiting transparency and human oversight. We present HiLSVA, a human-in-the-loop agentic system that supports mixed-initiative SciVis workflows. HiLSVA integrates a plan-first multi-agent architecture with explicit human oversight, stepwise provenance tracking, and learn-at-test-time adaptation from user feedback. The system supports fluid handoff between humans and agents through both natural language and direct manipulation of visualizations, while sandboxed execution ensures safe, reproducible workflows. In doing so, HiLSVA reframes agentic SciVis as a collaborative process that augments, rather than replaces, human analytical reasoning. We evaluate HiLSVA through representative case studies and a controlled user study with twelve participants of varying expertise across multiple autonomy settings. Results show that mixed-initiative interaction improves task completion, user control, and workflow transparency across different levels of user expertise, while revealing a tradeoff between execution efficiency and human oversight. These findings highlight the importance of human-centered design in agentic SciVis and guide the development of future collaborative visualization systems. We encourage readers to explore our demo video, case studies, and source code at https://hilsva.github.io/.

</details>
